    "code": 'import os\nimport json\nimport requests\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\nfrom urllib.parse import urljoin\nimport time\n\nprint(\'=== ANALYZING GOOGLE BOOKS CONTENT AND TRYING ITALIAN REPOSITORY ===\') \nprint(\'Objective: Extract dissertation content from Google Books pages and try the Italian thesis repository\\n\')\n\n# First, let\'s examine what files we have in workspace\nworkspace_files = os.listdir(\'workspace\')\nprint(f\'Available files in workspace: {workspace_files}\\n\')\n\n# Check if we have the Google Books HTML files\ngoogle_books_files = [f for f in workspace_files if \'google_books_response\' in f]\nprint(f\'Google Books HTML files found: {google_books_files}\')\n\nif google_books_files:\n    print(\'\\n=== ANALYZING GOOGLE BOOKS CONTENT FOR DISSERTATION REFERENCES ===\')\n    \n    for i, gb_file in enumerate(google_books_files, 1):\n        print(f\'\\n--- Analyzing Google Books file {i}: {gb_file} ---\')\n        \n        try:\n            with open(f\'workspace/{gb_file}\', \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                gb_content = f.read()\n            \n            print(f\'File size: {len(gb_content):,} characters\')\n            \n            # Parse the HTML content\n            soup = BeautifulSoup(gb_content, \'html.parser\')\n            \n            # Look for book title and metadata\n            title_elem = soup.find(\'title\')\n            if title_elem:\n                print(f\'Page title: {title_elem.get_text().strip()}\')\n            \n            # Search for key terms related to Lauria\'s dissertation\n            content_text = soup.get_text().lower()\n            \n            # Key terms to search for\n            search_terms = [\n                \'federico lauria\',\n                \'lauria\',\n                \'dissertation\', \n                \'thesis\',\n                \'2014\',\n                \'logic of the liver\',\n                \'deontic view\',\n                \'intentionality of desire\',\n                \'footnote 397\',\n                \'footnote\',\n                \'note 397\'\n            ]\n            \n            found_terms = {}\n            for term in search_terms:\n                count = content_text.count(term)\n                if count > 0:\n                    found_terms[term] = count\n                    print(f\'✓ Found "{term}": {count} occurrences\')\n            \n            if found_terms:\n                print(f\'\\nTotal relevant terms found: {len(found_terms)}\')\n                \n                # Extract passages containing the most relevant terms\n                if \'lauria\' in found_terms or \'federico lauria\' in found_terms:\n                    print(\'\\n--- EXTRACTING LAURIA REFERENCES ---\')\n                    \n                    # Find all text containing "lauria"\n                    text_content = soup.get_text()\n                    lauria_positions = []\n                    \n                    # Find all positions where "lauria" appears\n                    start = 0\n                    while True:\n                        pos = text_content.lower().find(\'lauria\', start)\n                        if pos == -1:\n                            break\n                        lauria_positions.append(pos)\n                        start = pos + 1\n                    \n                    print(f\'Found {len(lauria_positions)} "Lauria" references\')\n                    \n                    # Extract context around each reference\n                    for j, pos in enumerate(lauria_positions[:5], 1):  # Show first 5\n                        context_start = max(0, pos - 300)\n                        context_end = min(len(text_content), pos + 400)\n                        context = text_content[context_start:context_end]\n                        \n                        print(f\'\\nLauria Reference {j} (position {pos}):\')\n                        print(\'=\' * 80)\n                        print(context.strip())\n                        print(\'=\' * 80)\n                        \n                        # Check if this context mentions footnotes or specific years\n                        context_lower = context.lower()\n                        if \'2014\' in context_lower:\n                            print(\'*** Contains 2014 - potentially relevant! ***\')\n                        if \'footnote\' in context_lower or \'note\' in context_lower:\n                            print(\'*** Contains footnote reference - highly relevant! ***\')\n                        if \'dissertation\' in context_lower or \'thesis\' in context_lower:\n                            print(\'*** Contains dissertation reference - very relevant! ***\')\n                \n                # Look specifically for footnote references\n                if \'footnote\' in found_terms:\n                    print(\'\\n--- EXTRACTING FOOTNOTE REFERENCES ---\')\n                    \n                    footnote_positions = []\n                    start = 0\n                    while True:\n                        pos = text_content.lower().find(\'footnote\', start)\n                        if pos == -1:\n                            break\n                        footnote_positions.append(pos)\n                        start = pos + 1\n                    \n                    for j, pos in enumerate(footnote_positions[:3], 1):  # Show first 3\n                        context_start = max(0, pos - 200)\n                        context_end = min(len(text_content), pos + 300)\n                        context = text_content[context_start:context_end]\n                        \n                        print(f\'\\nFootnote Reference {j}:\')\n                        print(\'-\' * 60)\n                        print(context.strip())\n                        print(\'-\' * 60)\n                        \n                        # Check for number 397 specifically\n                        if \'397\' in context:\n                            print(\'🎯 *** FOOTNOTE 397 FOUND! ***\')\n            \n            else:\n                print(\'No relevant terms found in this Google Books page\')\n                print(f\'Content preview (first 500 chars): {content_text[:500]}...\')\n        \n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\'Error analyzing {gb_file}: {str(e)}\')\n\nprint(\'\\n=== ATTEMPTING TO ACCESS ITALIAN THESIS REPOSITORY ===\') \n\n# Try the Italian repository link that wasn\'t attempted before\nitalian_repo_url = \'https://tesidottorato.depositolegale.it/bitstream/20.500.14242/169480/1/conv_polito_thesis_Lauria.pdf\'\nprint(f\'Accessing Italian repository: {italian_repo_url}\')\n\n# Note: This is actually Anna Lauria\'s 2023 thesis, not Federico\'s, but let\'s check if accessible\nheaders = {\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/120.0.0.0 Safari/537.36\',\n    \'Accept\': \'application/pdf,text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,*/*;q=0.8\',\n    \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.9,it;q=0.8\'\n}\n\ntry:\n    italian_response = requests.get(italian_repo_url, headers=headers, timeout=30)\n    print(f\'Italian repository response status: {italian_response.status_code}\')\n    print(f\'Content type: {italian_response.headers.get("content-type", "unknown")}\')\n    print(f\'Content length: {len(italian_response.content):,} bytes\')\n    \n    if italian_response.status_code == 200:\n        content_type = italian_response.headers.get(\'content-type\', \'\').lower()\n        \n        if \'pdf\' in content_type and len(italian_response.content) > 100000:\n            # This is a PDF - save it for reference\n            pdf_path = \'workspace/anna_lauria_2023_thesis.pdf\'\n            with open(pdf_path, \'wb\') as pdf_file:\n                pdf_file.write(italian_response.content)\n            \n            file_size = os.path.getsize(pdf_path)\n            print(f\'\\n*** PDF DOWNLOADED FROM ITALIAN REPOSITORY ***\')\n            print(f\'Saved to: {pdf_path}\')\n            print(f\'File size: {file_size:,} bytes ({file_size/1024/1024:.2f} MB)\')\n            print(\'Note: This appears to be Anna Lauria\\\'s 2023 thesis, not Federico\\\'s 2014 dissertation\')\n            \n        elif \'html\' in content_type:\n            print(\'Received HTML response - may be an access page or redirect\')\n            # Save for analysis\n            with open(\'workspace/italian_repo_response.html\', \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                f.write(italian_response.text)\n            print(\'HTML response saved to workspace/italian_repo_response.html\')\n    \n    else:\n        print(f\'Italian repository access failed: {italian_response.status_code}\')\n        \nexcept Exception as e:\n    print(f\'Error accessing Italian repository: {str(e)}\')\n\nprint(\'\\n=== TRYING DIRECT SEARCH FOR FEDERICO LAURIA 2014 DISSERTATION ===\') \n\n# Try more specific searches for the actual dissertation\nsearch_queries = [\n    \'"Federico Lauria" "The Logic of the Liver" 2014 filetype:pdf\',\n    \'"Federico Lauria" dissertation 2014 "footnote 397"\',\n    \'"Logic of the Liver" "Deontic View" Lauria 2014 pdf\',\n    \'Federico Lauria PhD thesis 2014 Geneva Switzerland\'\n]\n\nfor i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1):\n    print(f\'\\n--- Search Query {i}: {query} ---\')\n    \n    try:\n        # Use Google search\n        search_url = f\'https://www.google.com/search?q={requests.utils.quote(query)}\'\n        print(f\'Search URL: {search_url[:100]}...\')\n        \n        search_response = requests.get(search_url, headers=headers, timeout=20)\n        print(f\'Search response status: {search_response.status_code}\')\n        \n        if search_response.status_code == 200:\n            search_soup = BeautifulSoup(search_response.content, \'html.parser\')\n            \n            # Look for search results\n            result_divs = search_soup.find_all(\'div\', class_=\'g\')\n            print(f\'Found {len(result_divs)} search results\')\n            \n            relevant_results = []\n            for result in result_divs[:5]:  # Check top 5 results\n                title_elem = result.find(\'h3\')\n                if title_elem:\n                    title_link = title_elem.find(\'a\')\n                    title = title_link.get_text().strip() if title_link else \'No title\'\n                    url = title_link.get(\'href\') if title_link else None\n                    \n                    snippet_elem = result.find(\'span\', class_=\'st\') or result.find(\'div\', class_=\'s\')\n                    snippet = snippet_elem.get_text().strip() if snippet_elem else \'No snippet\'\n                    \n                    # Check relevance\n                    combined_text = (title + snippet).lower()\n                    if (\'lauria\' in combined_text and \n                        (\'2014\' in combined_text or \'dissertation\' in combined_text or \'thesis\' in combined_text)):\n                        \n                        print(f\'  ✓ Relevant result: {title[:80]}...\')\n                        print(f\'    URL: {url}\')\n                        print(f\'    Snippet: {snippet[:150]}...\')\n                        \n                        relevant_results.append({\n                            \'title\': title,\n                            \'url\': url,\n                            \'snippet\': snippet,\n                            \'query\': query\n                        })\n            \n            if relevant_results:\n                print(f\'Found {len(relevant_results)} relevant results for this query\')\n            else:\n                print(\'No highly relevant results found for this query\')\n        \n        time.sleep(2)  # Rate limiting\n        \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\'Error with search query {i}: {str(e)}\')\n\nprint(\'\\n=== COMPREHENSIVE ANALYSIS SUMMARY ===\')\n\n# Check what we\'ve accomplished\nanalysis_summary = {\n    \'google_books_analyzed\': len(google_books_files),\n    \'italian_repo_attempted\': True,\n    \'search_queries_tried\': len(search_queries),\n    \'files_in_workspace\': len(workspace_files),\n    \'analysis_timestamp\': time.strftime(\'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S\')\n}\n\n# Save analysis summary\nwith open(\'workspace/dissertation_search_analysis.json\', \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n    json.dump(analysis_summary, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)\n\nprint(f\'\\n*** ANALYSIS COMPLETE ***\')\nprint(f\'✓ Analyzed {len(google_books_files)} Google Books HTML files\')\nprint(f\'✓ Attempted Italian repository access\')\nprint(f\'✓ Tried {len(search_queries)} specific search queries\')\nprint(f\'✓ Analysis summary saved to: workspace/dissertation_search_analysis.json\')\n\nprint(\'\\n🎯 KEY FINDINGS:\')\nif google_books_files:\n    print(\'- Google Books pages contain potential Lauria references\')\n    print(\'- Need to examine extracted content for footnote 397 specifically\')\nelse:\n    print(\'- No Google Books content available for analysis\')\n\nprint(\'\\n📋 NEXT STEPS NEEDED:\')\nprint(\'1. Consider contacting Federico Lauria directly or his institution\')\nprint(\'4. Look for secondary sources that might cite footnote 397\')\n\nprint(\'\\nObjective: Find Federico Lauria\\\'s 2014 dissertation and access footnote 397\')\nprint(\'Status: Analyzed available sources and attempted additional access methods\')',

first 5 occurrences\n                    context_start = max(0, pos - 500)\n                    context_end = min(len(full_text), pos + 600)\n                    context = full_text[context_start:context_end]\n                    \n                    print(f\'\\nOccurrence {j} of "{term}" (position {pos}):\')  \n                    print(\'─\' * 100)\n     "code": 'import os\nimport requests\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\nimport json\nimport time\nfrom urllib.parse import urljoin, quote\nimport re\n\nprint(\'=== SEARCHING SMITHSONIAN AMERICAN ART MUSEUM FOR LITERARY QUOTATION TITLES ===\')\nprint(\'Objective: Find paintings with titles that appear to be quotes from the same literary work\')\nprint(\'Focus: Paintings from August 2023 or earlier with chapter-based, numbered, or related quote titles\\n\')\n\n# Ensure workspace directory exists\nos.makedirs(\'workspace\', exist_ok=True)\n\n# Smithsonian American Art Museum collection search base URL\nbase_url = \'https://americanart.si.edu\'\nsearch_url = f\'{base_url}/collections/search\'\n\nheaders = {\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/120.0.0.0 Safari/537.36\',\n    \'Accept\': \'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8\',\n    \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.9\',\n    \'Accept-Encoding\': \'gzip, deflate, br\',\n    \'Connection\': \'keep-alive\',\n    \'Upgrade-Insecure-Requests\': \'1\'\n}\n\nprint(\'=== STEP 1: ACCESSING SMITHSONIAN COLLECTION SEARCH ===\\n\')\n\ntry:\n    # First, access the main search page to understand the structure\n    print(f\'Accessing: {search_url}\')\n    response = requests.get(search_url, headers=headers, timeout=30)\n    print(f\'Response status: {response.status_code}\')\n    print(f\'Content length: {len(response.content):,} bytes\')\n    \n    if response.status_code == 200:\n        soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, \'html.parser\')\n        \n        # Save the search page for analysis\n        with open(\'workspace/smithsonian_search_page.html\', \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n            f.write(response.text)\n        print(\'✓ Search page saved to workspace/smithsonian_search_page.html\')\n        \n        # Look for search form and parameters\n        search_forms = soup.find_all(\'form\')\n        print(f\'Found {len(search_forms)} forms on the page\')\n        \n        # Look for any existing search parameters or filters\n        input_fields = soup.find_all(\'input\')\n        select_fields = soup.find_all(\'select\')\n        \n        print(f\'Found {len(input_fields)} input fields and {len(select_fields)} select fields\')\n        \n        # Try to identify the search mechanism\n        search_inputs = [inp for inp in input_fields if inp.get(\'name\') and \n                        any(term in inp.get(\'name\', \'\').lower() for term in [\'search\', \'query\', \'q\', \'term\'])]\n        \n        if search_inputs:\n            print(f\'Identified {len(search_inputs)} search input fields:\')\n            for inp in search_inputs:\n                print(f\'  - {inp.get("name")}: {inp.get("type", "text")}\')\n        \n        print(\'\\n=== STEP 2: SEARCHING FOR PAINTINGS WITH QUOTATION-LIKE TITLES ===\\n\')\n        \n        # Strategy: Search for common patterns in literary quotation titles\n        quotation_patterns = [\n            \'Chapter\',  # Chapter-based titles\n            \'Book\',     # Book references\n            \'Canto\',    # Poetry cantos\n            \'Part\',     # Part references\n            \'Volume\',   # Volume references\n            \'Verse\',    # Verse references\n            \'Stanza\',   # Stanza references\n            \'Act\',      # Play acts\n            \'Scene\',    # Play scenes\n            \'Line\',     # Line references\n            \'Page\',     # Page references\n            \'Passage\',  # Passage references\n        ]\n        \n        # Also search for numbered titles that might indicate sequential quotes\n        numbered_patterns = [\n            \'I.\',       # Roman numerals\n            \'II.\',\n            \'III.\',\n            \'IV.\',\n            \'V.\',\n            \'VI.\',\n            \'VII.\',\n            \'VIII.\',\n            \'IX.\',\n            \'X.\',\n            \'1.\',       # Arabic numerals\n            \'2.\',\n            \'3.\',\n            \'4.\',\n            \'5.\',\n            \'First\',    # Written numbers\n            \'Second\',\n            \'Third\',\n            \'Fourth\',\n            \'Fifth\'\n        ]\n        \n        all_search_results = []\n        \n        # Search for each pattern\n        search_terms = quotation_patterns + numbered_patterns\n        \n        for i, term in enumerate(search_terms, 1):\n            print(f\'--- Search {i}/{len(search_terms)}: "{term}" ---\')\n            \n            try:\n                # Construct search URL - try different approaches\n                search_params = {\n                    \'q\': term,\n                    \'search\': term\n                }\n                \n                # Try the most likely search parameter\n                search_query_url = f\'{search_url}?q={quote(term)}\'\n                print(f\'Trying: {search_query_url}\')\n                \n                search_response = requests.get(search_query_url, headers=headers, timeout=20)\n                print(f\'Search response status: {search_response.status_code}\')\n                \n                if search_response.status_code == 200:\n                    search_soup = BeautifulSoup(search_response.content, \'html.parser\')\n                    \n                    # Look for artwork results\n                    # Common patterns for museum search results\n                    result_selectors = [\n                        \'.search-result\',\n                        \'.artwork\',\n                        \'.collection-item\',\n                        \'.result-item\',\n                        \'.object\',\n                        \'.artwork-item\',\n                        \'article\',\n                        \'.card\'\n                    ]\n                    \n                    results_found = []\n                    \n                    for selector in result_selectors:\n                        results = search_soup.select(selector)\n                        if results:\n                            print(f\'  Found {len(results)} results using selector: {selector}\')\n                            results_found.extend(results)\n                            break\n                    \n                    if not results_found:\n                        # Try to find any links that might be artwork results\n                        all_links = search_soup.find_all(\'a\', href=True)\n                        artwork_links = []\n                        \n                        for link in all_links:\n                            href = link.get(\'href\', \'\')\n                            text = link.get_text().strip()\n                            \n                            # Look for links that might be artworks\n                            if ((\'/artwork/\' in href or \'/object/\' in href or \'/collection/\' in href) and \n                                len(text) > 5 and text != \'View\' and text != \'More\'):\n                                artwork_links.append({\n                                    \'title\': text,\n                                    \'url\': urljoin(base_url, href),\n                                    \'search_term\': term\n                                })\n                        \n                        if artwork_links:\n                            print(f\'  Found {len(artwork_links)} potential artwork links\')\n                            results_found = artwork_links\n                    \n                    # Process found results\n                    if results_found:\n                        for j, result in enumerate(results_found[:10], 1):  # Limit to first 10 results\n                            if isinstance(result, dict):  # It\'s already processed\n                                title = result[\'title\']\n                                url = result[\'url\']\n                            else:  # It\'s a BeautifulSoup element\n                                title_elem = result.find([\'h1\', \'h2\', \'h3\', \'h4\', \'title\', \'a\'])\n                                title = title_elem.get_text().strip() if title_elem else \'No title found\'\n                                \n                                link_elem = result.find(\'a\', href=True)\n                                url = urljoin(base_url, link_elem.get(\'href\')) if link_elem else None\n                            \n                            print(f\'    {j}. {title[:80]}...\')\n                            if url:\n                                print(f\'       URL: {url}\')\n                            \n                            # Check if this title looks like a literary quotation\n                            title_lower = title.lower()\n                            quotation_indicators = [\n                                \'chapter\', \'book\', \'canto\', \'part\', \'volume\', \'verse\', \'stanza\',\n                                \'act\', \'scene\', \'line\', \'page\', \'passage\', \'from\', \'after\',\n                                \'i.\', \'ii.\', \'iii.\', \'iv.\', \'v.\', \'first\', \'second\', \'third\'\n                            ]\n                            \n                            is_potential_quote = any(indicator in title_lower for indicator in quotation_indicators)\n                            \n                            if is_potential_quote:\n                                print(f\'       *** POTENTIAL LITERARY QUOTATION TITLE ***\')\n                                \n                                all_search_results.append({\n                                    \'title\': title,\n                                    \'url\': url,\n                                    \'search_term\': term,\n                                    \'potential_quotation\': True,\n                                    \'quotation_indicators\': [ind for ind in quotation_indicators if ind in title_lower]\n                                })\n                    else:\n                        print(f\'  No results found for "{term}"\')\n                \n                else:\n                    print(f\'  Search failed with status: {search_response.status_code}\')\n                \n                # Rate limiting\n                time.sleep(1.5)\n                \n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f\'  Error searching for "{term}": {str(e)}\')\n        \n        print(f\'\\n=== STEP 3: ANALYZING POTENTIAL LITERARY QUOTATION TITLES ===\\n\')\n        \n        if all_search_results:\n            print(f\'Found {len(all_search_results)} potential literary quotation titles:\')\n            \n            # Group results by similar patterns to identify potential series\n            title_groups = {}\n            \n            for result in all_search_results:\n                title = result[\'title\']\n                \n                # Extract potential source patterns\n                # Look for common words that might indicate the same source\n                words = re.findall(r\'\\b[A-Z][a-z]+\\b\', title)  # Capitalized words\n                \n                # Create grouping key based on common patterns\n                key_words = []\n                for word in words:\n                    if word.lower() not in [\'the\', \'and\', \'or\', \'but\', \'in\', \'on\', \'at\', \'to\', \'for\', \'of\', \'with\', \'by\']:\n                        key_words.append(word.lower())\n                \n                # Group by first few significant words\n                if key_words:\n                    group_key = \' \'.join(key_words[:3])  # First 3 significant words\n                    if group_key not in title_groups:\n                        title_groups[group_key] = []\n                    title_groups[group_key].append(result)\n            \n            print(f\'\\nGrouped into {len(title_groups)} potential title families:\')\n            \n            promising_groups = []\n            \n            for group_key, group_results in title_groups.items():\n                if len(group_results) >= 2:  # Groups with multiple similar titles\n                    print(f\'\\n*** GROUP: "{group_key}" ({len(group_results)} titles) ***\')\n                    promising_groups.append({\n                        \'group_key\': group_key,\n                        \'count\': len(group_results),\n                        \'titles\': group_results\n                    })\n                    \n                    for result in group_results:\n                        print(f\'  - {result["title"]}\')\n                        if result.get(\'url\'):\n                            print(f\'    URL: {result["url"]}\')\n                        print(f\'    Indicators: {result.get("quotation_indicators", [])}\')\n            \n            # Save all results\n            search_summary = {\n                \'search_timestamp\': time.strftime(\'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S\'),\n                \'total_search_terms\': len(search_terms),\n                \'total_results_found\': len(all_search_results),\n                \'potential_quotation_titles\': all_search_results,\n                \'title_groups\': title_groups,\n                \'promising_groups\': promising_groups,\n                \'search_objective\': \'Find paintings with titles that appear to be quotes from the same literary work\'\n            }\n            \n            with open(\'workspace/smithsonian_literary_quotation_search.json\', \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                json.dump(search_summary, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)\n            \n            print(f\'\\n✓ Search results saved to: workspace/smithsonian_literary_quotation_search.json\')\n            \n            if promising_groups:\n                print(f\'\\n🎯 MOST PROMISING FINDINGS:\')\n                \n                # Sort groups by count (most titles first)\n                promising_groups.sort(key=lambda x: x[\'count\'], reverse=True)\n                \n                for i, group in enumerate(promising_groups[:3], 1):  # Top 3 groups\n                    print(f\'\\n{i}. GROUP "{group["group_key"]}" - {group["count"]} related titles:\')\n                    \n                    for title_result in group[\'titles\']:\n                        print(f\'   • {title_result["title"]}\')\n                    \n                    print(f\'   → This group suggests paintings that may quote from the same literary source\')\n                \n                print(f\'\\n📋 NEXT STEPS:\')\n                print(\'1. Analyze the complete titles and descriptions for literary source identification\')\n                print(\'4. Look for artist statements or curatorial notes that might identify the source text\')\n                \n            else:\n                print(f\'\\n⚠ No clear title groups found - titles appear to be from different sources\')\n                print(\'Individual titles found may still be literary quotations but from different works\')\n        \n        else:\n            print(\'No potential literary quotation titles found in the search results\')\n            print(\'\\nThis could mean:\')\n            print(\'1. The collection search requires different search terms or approaches\')\n    \n    else:\n        print(f\'Failed to access Smithsonian search page: {response.status_code}\')\n        print(f\'Response preview: {response.text[:500]}...\')\n\nexcept Exception as e:\n    print(f\'Error accessing Smithsonian American Art Museum: {str(e)}\')\n    import traceback\n    traceback.print_exc()\n\nprint(\'\\n=== SMITHSONIAN SEARCH COMPLETE ===\')\nprint(\'Objective: Identify paintings with titles that appear to be quotes from the same literary work\')\nprint(\'Status: Search completed - results saved to workspace for further analysis\')',

class="flex items-center azalea-heading-level-6"><div class="mr-1.5 text-black"><div aria-hidden="true" class="fill-current w-3 h-3 md:w-4 md:h-4"><svg class="icon" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" viewbox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0h24v24H0z" fill="none" stroke="none"></path><line x1="3" x2="21" y1="21" y2="21"></line><line x1="3" x2="21" y1="10" y2="10"></line><polyline points="5 6 12 3 19 6"></polyline><line x1="4" x2="4" y1="10" y2="21"></line><line x1="20" x2="20" y1="10" y2="21"></line><line x1="8" x2="8" y1="14" y2="17"></line><line x1="12" x2="12" y1="14" y2="17"></line><line x1="16" x2="16" y1="14" y2="17"></line></svg></div></div><a class="text-black hover:no-underline" href="/visit/saam ">Smithsonian American Art Museum</a></div><div class="azalea-text-sm text-black">\n            SAAM\'s groundbreaking exhibition examines the ways in which American sculpture has shaped and reflected attitudes and understandings about race in the United States. \n          </div></div></div><footer class="pb-4 text-left"></footer></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="azalea-container"><div class="views-element-container drupal-block azalea-container"     </div></header><div class="azalea-text-sm pb-4 text-tertiary-900"><div class="azalea-text-sm">\n          SAAM’s collection includes many remarkable artworks that reflect the profound and longstanding contributions of Asian American and Asian diasporic artists in the United States. \n        </div></div></a></div></div><div class=""><div><a aria-label="Photography" class="azalea-card @container flex flex-col overflow-hidden rounded-sm w-full hover:no-underline" href="/art/highlights/photography" rel="bookmark"><div class="flex w-full mb-4"><picture class="w-full"><img alt="A portrait of a man with goatee contained in a brooch" class="mx-auto max-h-80 md:max-h-96 lg:max-h-128 azalea-alt-text-sr-only" loading="lazy" title=""/></picture></div><header class="pb-4 font-heading font-bold text-tertiary-900 text-xl"><div class="azalea-heading-level-4 text-black">\n                      Photography\n                  </div></header><div class="azalea-text-sm pb-4 text-tertiary-900"><div class="azalea-text-sm">\n          In 1983, the Smithsonian American Art Museum began actively building its photography collection. That year, more than 1,500 photographs were transferred to the museum from the National Endowment for the Arts. Since then, the collection has grown to more than 9,000 works that span the history of the medium. \n        </div></div></a></div></div><div class=""><div><a aria-label="Latinx Art" class="azalea-card @container flex flex-col overflow-hidden rounded-sm w-full hover:no-underline" href="/art/highlights/latinx" rel="bookmark"><div class="flex w-full mb-4"><picture class="w-full"><img alt="Media - 2020.25.1 - SAAM-2020.25.1_1 - 138936" class="mx-auto max-h-80 md:max-h-96 lg:max-h-128 azalea-alt-text-sr-only" loading="lazy" src="//cdn.saam.media/a3o_nVhKGrSVJUEiYWsNAA5-ZpI/640/0/center/cover/jpg/https%3A%2F%2Fd3ec1vt3scx7rr.cloudfront.net%2Ffiles%2Fartwork%2Fimages%2FSAAM-2020.25.1_1.jpg" title=""/></picture></div><header class="pb-4 font-heading font-bold text-tertiary-900 text-xl"><div class="azalea-heading-level-4 text-black">\n                      Latinx Art\n                  </div></header><div class="azalea-text-sm pb-4 text-tertiary-900"><div class="azalea-text-sm">\n          The Smithsonian American Art Museum’s leading Latinx art collection represents a profound commitment to building a great national collection reflecting the rich contributions of Latinos to our country, from the colonial period to the present.\n        </div></div></a></div></div><div class=""><div><a aria-label="Sculpture" class="azalea-card @container flex flex-col overflow-hidden rounded-sm w-full hover:no-underline" href="/art/highlights/sculpture" rel="bookmark"><div title=""/></picture></div><header class="pb-4 font-heading font-bold text-tertiary-900 text-xl"><div class="azalea-heading-level-4 text-black">\n                      Sculpture\n                  </div></header><div class="azalea-text-sm pb-4 text-tertiary-900"><div class="azalea-text-sm">\n          The museum’s American sculpture collection is one of the largest and most comprehensive in the world.\n        </div></div></a></div></div><div class=""><div><a aria-label="Contemporary Art" class="azalea-card @container flex flex-col overflow-hidden rounded-sm w-full hover:no-underline" title=""/></picture></div><header class="pb-4 font-heading font-bold text-tertiary-900 text-xl"><div class="azalea-heading-level-4 text-black">\n                      Contemporary Art\n                  </div></header><div class="azalea-text-sm pb-4 text-tertiary-900"><div class="azalea-text-sm">\n          Contemporary Art\r\n\n        </div></div></a></div></div><div class=""><div><a class="azalea-text-sm pb-4 text-tertiary-900"><div class="azalea-text-sm">\n          The Time-Based Media Art Initiative at the Smithsonian American Art Museum reflects a commitment to develop the museum’s time-based media collections, research resources, and programs.\n        </div></div></a></div></div><div class=""><div><a aria-label="19th Century" class="azalea-card @container flex largest collections from the last quarter of the nineteenth century, including impressionist and Gilded Age works.\n        </div></div></a></div></div><div class=""><div><a aria-label="20th Century" class="azalea-card @container flex flex-col overflow-hidden rounded-sm w-full hover:no-underline" href="/art/highlights/20th-century" rel="bookmark"><div class="flex w-full mb-4"><picture class="ordinal">th</sup> Century\n                  </div></header><div class="azalea-text-sm pb-4 text-tertiary-900"><div class="azalea-text-sm">\n          Artists in the twentieth century chose two distinct ways to depict modernism and the excitement of progress—realism and abstraction. Both are well represented in the collection. The museum has the largest collection of New Deal art and murals in the country.\n        </div></div></a></div></div><div class=""><div><a aria-label="African American Art" class="azalea-card title=""/></picture></div><header class="pb-4 font-heading font-bold text-tertiary-900 text-xl"><div class="azalea-heading-level-4 text-black">\n                      African American Art\n                  </div></header><div class="azalea-text-sm pb-4 text-tertiary-900"><div class="azalea-text-sm">\n          SAAM is home to one of the most significant collections of works by African American artists in the world.\n        </div></div></a></div></div><div class=""><div><a aria-label="Native and Indigenous Art" class="azalea-card @container flex flex-col overflow-hidden rounded-sm w-full            </div></header><div class="azalea-text-sm pb-4 text-tertiary-900"><div class="azalea-text-sm">\n          SAAM is committed to collecting and sharing art by Native makers whose perspectives and experiences are shaping American culture and identity.\r\n\n        </div></div></a></div></div><div class=""><div><a aria-label="Contemporary Craft and Decorative Arts" class="azalea-card one of the finest in the United States.\n        </div></div></a></div></div><div class=""><div><a aria-label="Folk and Self-Taught Art" class="azalea-card @container flex flex-col overflow-hidden title=""/></picture></div><header class="pb-4 font-heading font-bold text-tertiary-900 text-xl"><div class="azalea-heading-level-4 text-black">\n                      Folk and Self-Taught Art\n                  </div></header><div class="azalea-text-sm pb-4 text-tertiary-900"><div class="azalea-text-sm">\n          The Smithsonian American Art Museum’s collection of folk and self-taught art represents the powerful vision of America’s untrained and vernacular artists. SAAM is one of the only major museums to clearly advocate for a diverse populist and uniquely American voice within the context of what is traditionally considered great art.  \n        </div></div></a></div></div><div class=""><div><a aria-label="Works on Paper" class="azalea-card @container flex flex-col overflow-hidden rounded-sm w-full hover:no-underline" class="pb-4 font-heading font-bold text-tertiary-900 text-xl"><div class="azalea-heading-level-4 text-black">\n                      Works on\xa0Paper\n                  </div></header><div class="azalea-text-sm pb-4 text-tertiary-900"><div class="azalea-text-sm">\n          Graphic arts comprise a large part of the museum’s collection, which reveals the central importance of works on paper for American artists, both as studies for creations in other media and as finished works of art. \n        </div></div></a></div></div><div class=""><div><a aria-label="Early American Art" class="azalea-card @container flex flex-col overflow-hidden rounded-sm w-full hover:no-underline" href="/art/highlights/early-america" rel="bookmark"><div class="flex w-full mb-4"><picture class="azalea-text-sm pb-4 text-tertiary-900"><div class="azalea-text-sm">\n          The museum’s collection begins with works from the colonies of New Spain and New England. \n     "code": 'import os\nimport json\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\nimport requests\nfrom urllib.parse import urljoin, quote\nimport time\nimport re\n\nprint(\'=== ANALYZING SMITHSONIAN SEARCH PAGE AND TRYING DIRECT BROWSE APPROACH ===\')\nprint(\'Objective: Understand the search mechanism and find paintings with literary quotation titles\\n\')\n\n# First, let\'s inspect the saved search page to understand the structure\nsearch_page_file = \'workspace/smithsonian_search_page.html\'\n\nif os.path.exists(search_page_file):\n    print(\'=== ANALYZING SAVED SEARCH PAGE HTML ===\')\n    \n    with open(search_page_file, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n        search_html = f.read()\n    \n    print(f\'Search page HTML size: {len(search_html):,} characters\')\n    \n    soup = BeautifulSoup(search_html, \'html.parser\')\n    \n    # Look for the actual search form structure\n    print(\'\\n--- ANALYZING SEARCH FORM STRUCTURE ---\')\n    \n    forms = soup.find_all(\'form\')\n    print(f\'Found {len(forms)} forms\')\n    \n    for i, form in enumerate(forms, 1):\n        print(f\'\\nForm {i}:\')\n        print(f\'  Action: {form.get("action", "No action")}\')\n        print(f\'  Method: {form.get("method", "GET")}\')\n        \n        # Find all input fields in this form\n        inputs = form.find_all(\'input\')\n        selects = form.find_all(\'select\')\n        \n        print(f\'  Inputs: {len(inputs)}\')\n        for inp in inputs:\n            name = inp.get(\'name\', \'unnamed\')\n            input_type = inp.get(\'type\', \'text\')\n            value = inp.get(\'value\', \'\')\n            placeholder = inp.get(\'placeholder\', \'\')\n            print(f\'    - {name} ({input_type}): value="{value}" placeholder="{placeholder}"\')\n        \n        print(f\'  Selects: {len(selects)}\')\n        for sel in selects:\n            name = sel.get(\'name\', \'unnamed\')\n            options = sel.find_all(\'option\')\n            print(f\'    - {name}: {len(options)} options\')\n    \n    # Look for any JavaScript or AJAX search mechanisms\n    print(\'\\n--- LOOKING FOR JAVASCRIPT SEARCH MECHANISMS ---\')\n    scripts = soup.find_all(\'script\')\n    print(f\'Found {len(scripts)} script tags\')\n    \n    # Look for any data attributes or API endpoints\n    elements_with_data = soup.find_all(attrs={\'data-url\': True})\n    if elements_with_data:\n        print(\'\\nElements with data-url attributes:\')\n        for elem in elements_with_data[:5]:  # Show first 5\n            print(f\'  - {elem.name}: {elem.get("data-url")}\')\n    \n    # Look for browse artwork links that might be more useful\n    print(\'\\n--- FINDING BROWSE ARTWORK LINKS ---\')\n    browse_links = []\n    \n    for link in soup.find_all(\'a\', href=True):\n        href = link.get(\'href\')\n        text = link.get_text().strip()\n        \n        if (\'browse\' in text.lower() or \'artwork\' in href.lower() or \n            \'collection\' in href.lower()) and len(text) > 3:\n            browse_links.append({\n                \'text\': text,\n                \'href\': href,\n                \'full_url\': urljoin(\'https://americanart.si.edu\', href)\n            })\n    \n    print(f\'Found {len(browse_links)} browse/artwork links:\')\n    for link in browse_links[:10]:  # Show first 10\n        print(f\'  - "{link["text"]}" -> {link["href"]}\')\nelse:\n    print(\'❌ Search page HTML file not found\')\n\nprint(\'\\n=== TRYING DIRECT BROWSE ARTWORK APPROACH ===\')\n\n# Try the direct browse artwork URL that appeared in search results\nbrowse_url = \'https://americanart.si.edu/search/artworks?content_type=artwork\'\nprint(f\'Accessing browse artwork page: {browse_url}\')\n\nheaders = {\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/120.0.0.0 Safari/537.36\',\n    \'Accept\': \'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8\',\n    \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.9\',\n    \'Accept-Encoding\': \'gzip, deflate, br\',\n    \'Connection\': \'keep-alive\',\n    \'Upgrade-Insecure-Requests\': \'1\'\n}\n\ntry:\n    browse_response = requests.get(browse_url, headers=headers, timeout=30)\n    print(f\'Browse response status: {browse_response.status_code}\')\n    print(f\'Content length: {len(browse_response.content):,} bytes\')\n    \n    if browse_response.status_code == 200:\n        # Save the browse page for analysis\n        with open(\'workspace/smithsonian_browse_artworks.html\', \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n            f.write(browse_response.text)\n        print(\'✓ Browse artworks page saved to workspace/smithsonian_browse_artworks.html\')\n        \n        browse_soup = BeautifulSoup(browse_response.content, \'html.parser\')\n        \n        # Look for artwork items on the browse page\n        print(\'\\n--- ANALYZING BROWSE PAGE FOR ARTWORK ITEMS ---\')\n        \n        # Common selectors for artwork items\n        artwork_selectors = [\n            \'.artwork\',\n            \'.collection-item\',\n            \'.search-result\',\n            \'.result-item\',\n            \'.object\',\n            \'.card\',\n            \'article\',\n            \'[data-artwork]\',\n            \'.artwork-card\',\n            \'.item\'\n        ]\n        \n        artwork_items = []\n        \n        for selector in artwork_selectors:\n            items = browse_soup.select(selector)\n            if items and len(items) > 5:  # Only consider selectors with substantial results\n                print(f\'Found {len(items)} items using selector: {selector}\')\n                artwork_items = items\n                break\n        \n        if artwork_items:\n            print(f\'\\n--- ANALYZING FIRST 10 ARTWORK ITEMS ---\')\n            \n            potential_quotes = []\n            \n            for i, item in enumerate(artwork_items[:20], 1):  # Check first 20 items\n                # Try to extract title and link\n                title_elem = item.find([\'h1\', \'h2\', \'h3\', \'h4\', \'h5\', \'title\', \'a\'])\n                if title_elem:\n                    title = title_elem.get_text().strip()\n                    \n                    # Look for link to full artwork page\n                    link_elem = item.find(\'a\', href=True)\n                    link_url = None\n                    if link_elem:\n                        link_url = urljoin(\'https://americanart.si.edu\', link_elem.get(\'href\'))\n                    \n                    print(f\'{i:2d}. {title[:80]}...\')\n                    if link_url:\n                        print(f\'    URL: {link_url}\')\n                    \n                    # Check if this title looks like a literary quotation\n                    title_lower = title.lower()\n                    \n                    # Patterns that might indicate literary quotations\n                    literary_patterns = [\n                        r\'chapter\\s+\\d+\',\n                        r\'book\\s+\\d+\',\n                        r\'canto\\s+\\d+\',\n                        r\'part\\s+[ivx]+\',\n                        r\'volume\\s+\\d+\',\n                        r\'act\\s+[ivx]+\',\n                        r\'scene\\s+[ivx]+\',\n                        r\'\\b[ivx]+\\.\\s\',\n                        r\'\\b\\d+\\.\\s\',\n                        r\'from\\s+["\\\']\',\n                        r\'after\\s+["\\\']\',\n                        r\'["\\\'].+["\\\']\',  # Quoted text\n                        r\'first|second|third|fourth|fifth\',\n                        r\'\\bverse\\b\',\n                        r\'\\bstanza\\b\',\n                        r\'\\bline\\b.*\\d+\',\n                        r\'\\bpage\\b.*\\d+\'\n                    ]\n                    \n                    matches = []\n                    for pattern in literary_patterns:\n                        if re.search(pattern, title_lower):\n                            matches.append(pattern)\n                    \n                    if matches:\n                        print(f\'    *** POTENTIAL LITERARY QUOTATION ***\')\n                        print(f\'    Matched patterns: {matches}\')\n                        \n                        potential_quotes.append({\n                            \'title\': title,\n                            \'url\': link_url,\n                            \'patterns\': matches,\n                            \'position\': i\n                        })\n            \n            print(f\'\\n=== POTENTIAL LITERARY QUOTATION TITLES FOUND: {len(potential_quotes)} ===\')\n            \n            if potential_quotes:\n                for i, quote in enumerate(potential_quotes, 1):\n                    print(f\'\\n{i}. "{quote["title"]}"\')\n                    print(f\'   URL: {quote["url"]}\')\n                    print(f\'   Patterns: {quote["patterns"]}\')\n                \n                # Group similar titles to find series\n                print(\'\\n--- LOOKING FOR TITLE SERIES ---\')\n                \n                # Extract key words from titles to find groups\n                title_groups = {}\n                \n                for quote in potential_quotes:\n                    title = quote[\'title\']\n                    \n                    # Extract significant words (capitalized, longer than 3 chars)\n                    words = re.findall(r\'\\b[A-Z][a-z]{2,}\\b\', title)\n                    \n                    # Create grouping key from first few significant words\n                    if words:\n                        group_key = \' \'.join(words[:3]).lower()\n                        \n                        if group_key not in title_groups:\n                            title_groups[group_key] = []\n                        title_groups[group_key].append(quote)\n                \n                # Find groups with multiple titles (potential series)\n                series_groups = {k: v for k, v in title_groups.items() if len(v) >= 2}\n                \n                if series_groups:\n                    print(f\'Found {len(series_groups)} potential title series:\')\n                    \n                    for group_key, group_items in series_groups.items():\n                        print(f\'\\n*** SERIES: "{group_key}" ({len(group_items)} titles) ***\')\n                        for item in group_items:\n                            print(f\'  - {item["title"]}\')\n                        \n                        print(f\'  → These may be quotes from the same literary work\')\n                else:\n                    print(\'No clear title series found, but individual titles may still be literary quotations\')\n                \n                # Save results\n                results = {\n                    \'search_timestamp\': time.strftime(\'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S\'),\n                    \'browse_url\': browse_url,\n                    \'total_artworks_analyzed\': len(artwork_items),\n                    \'potential_literary_quotations\': potential_quotes,\n                    \'title_series\': series_groups,\n                    \'search_objective\': \'Find paintings with titles that appear to be quotes from the same literary work\'\n                }\n                \n                with open(\'workspace/smithsonian_literary_quotations_found.json\', \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                    json.dump(results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)\n                \n                print(f\'\\n✓ Results saved to: workspace/smithsonian_literary_quotations_found.json\')\n                \n            else:\n                print(\'No potential literary quotation titles found in the first 20 artworks\')\n        \n        else:\n            print(\'No artwork items found on browse page\')\n            \n            # Try to understand the page structure\n            print(\'\\n--- ANALYZING BROWSE PAGE STRUCTURE ---\')\n            \n            # Look for pagination or load more buttons\n            pagination = browse_soup.find_all([\'nav\', \'div\'], class_=re.compile(r\'pag|load|more\', re.I))\n            if pagination:\n                print(f\'Found {len(pagination)} pagination/load elements\')\n            \n            # Look for any search filters or parameters\n            filters = browse_soup.find_all([\'select\', \'input\'], attrs={\'name\': True})\n            if filters:\n                print(f\'Found {len(filters)} filter elements:\')\n                for filt in filters[:5]:\n                    print(f\'  - {filt.get("name")}: {filt.name}\')\n            \n            # Save page content preview for manual inspection\n            page_text = browse_soup.get_text()\n            preview = page_text[:2000]\n            print(f\'\\nPage content preview (first 2000 chars):\')\n            print(\'─\' * 80)\n            print(preview)\n            print(\'─\' * 80)\n    \n    else:\n        print(f\'Failed to access browse page: {browse_response.status_code}\')\n        print(f\'Response preview: {browse_response.text[:500]}...\')\n\nexcept Exception as e:\n    print(f\'Error accessing browse page: {str(e)}\')\n    import traceback\n    traceback.print_exc()\n\nprint(\'\\n=== TRYING ALTERNATIVE SEARCH APPROACHES ===\')\n\n# Try some specific search terms that might work better\nspecific_searches = [\n    \'title:Chapter\',\n    \'title:Book\',\n    \'title:"Chapter"\',\n    \'title:"from"\',\n    \'title:"after"\',\n    \'quotation\',\n    \'literary\',\n    \'poem\',\n    \'novel\',\n    \'verse\'\n]\n\nfor i, search_term in enumerate(specific_searches[:3], 1):  # Try first 3\n    print(f\'\\n--- Alternative Search {i}: "{search_term}" ---\')\n    \n    try:\n        # Try different search URL formats\n        search_urls = [\n            f\'https://americanart.si.edu/search/artworks?q={quote(search_term)}\',\n            f\'https://americanart.si.edu/collections/search?query={quote(search_term)}\',\n            f\'https://americanart.si.edu/search?q={quote(search_term)}&content_type=artwork\'\n        ]\n        \n        for j, search_url in enumerate(search_urls, 1):\n            print(f\'  Trying URL format {j}: {search_url[:80]}...\')\n            \n            search_response = requests.get(search_url, headers=headers, timeout=20)\n            print(f\'  Response status: {search_response.status_code}\')\n            \n            if search_response.status_code == 200:\n                search_soup = BeautifulSoup(search_response.content, \'html.parser\')\n                \n                # Look for actual search results (not the generic "Explore the Art" page)\n                page_text = search_soup.get_text().lower()\n                \n                if (\'explore the art\' in page_text and \n                    \'browse artwork\' in page_text and \n                    len(page_text) < 2000):\n                    print(f\'  → Generic page returned (same as before)\')\n                else:\n                    print(f\'  → Different content returned! ({len(page_text):,} chars)\')\n                    \n                    # Look for artwork results\n                    results = search_soup.find_all([\'article\', \'div\'], class_=re.compile(r\'result|artwork|item\', re.I))\n                    if results:\n                        print(f\'  Found {len(results)} potential results\')\n                        \n                        for k, result in enumerate(results[:3], 1):\n                            title_elem = result.find([\'h1\', \'h2\', \'h3\', \'h4\', \'a\'])\n                            if title_elem:\n                                title = title_elem.get_text().strip()\n                                print(f\'    {k}. {title[:60]}...\')\n                    break\n            \n            time.sleep(1)  # Rate limiting\n        \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\'  Error with search "{search_term}": {str(e)}\')\n    \n    time.sleep(2)  # Rate limiting between searches\n\nprint(\'\\n=== SMITHSONIAN ANALYSIS COMPLETE ===\')\nprint(\'Summary:\')\nprint(\'- Analyzed the search page structure\')\nprint(\'- Attempted direct browse approach\')\nprint(\'- Looked for artwork items with literary quotation patterns\')\nprint(\'- Tried alternative search URL formats\')\nprint(\'- Results saved to workspace for further analysis\')\n\nprint(\'\\nNext steps if literary quotations were found:\')\nprint(\'1. Access individual artwork pages for full details and dates\')\nprint(\'2. Verify which paintings are from August 2023 or earlier\')\nprint(\'3. Look for artist statements or descriptions that identify the source text\')\nprint(\'4. Group related titles to identify the common literary work\')',

This implementation: (1) First analyzes the saved search page HTML to understand the correct form structure, input fields, and search mechanisms, (2) Examines any JavaScript or AJAX search functionality that might explain why the previous searches failed, (3) Tries the direct 'Browse Artwork' approach using the URL that appeared in all search results, (4) Analyzes the browse page to identify actual artwork items using various CSS selectors, (5) For each artwork found, checks the title against literary quotation patterns using regex (Chapter X, Book X, Roman numerals, quoted text, etc.), (6) Groups similar titles to identify potential series from the same literary work, (7) Tries alternative search URL formats and parameters that might work better than the basic query approach, and (8) Saves all findings for further analysis. The goal is to identify paintings whose titles suggest they are quotes from the same literary source, which could help identify the work referenced in Federico Lauria's footnote 397 without needing direct access to the dissertation.",

    "code": 'import os\nimport json\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\nimport requests\nfrom urllib.parse import urljoin, quote\nimport time\nimport re\n\nprint(\'=== ANALYZING SMITHSONIAN BROWSE PAGE AND EXTRACTING ARTWORK DATA ===\')\nprint(\'Objective: Parse the saved browse page to find actual artwork titles and check for literary quotations\\n\')\n\n# First, let\'s inspect what files we have in workspace\nworkspace_files = [f for f in os.listdir(\'workspace\') if os.path.isfile(os.path.join(\'workspace\', f))]\nprint(f\'Files in workspace: {len(workspace_files)}\')\nfor file in workspace_files:\n    file_path = os.path.join(\'workspace\', file)\n    file_size = os.path.getsize(file_path)\n    print(f\'  - {file}: {file_size:,} bytes\')\n\n# Look for the browse artworks HTML file\nbrowse_file = \'workspace/smithsonian_browse_artworks.html\'\n\nif os.path.exists(browse_file):\n    print(f\'\\n=== ANALYZING BROWSE ARTWORKS PAGE ===\\n\')\n    \n    with open(browse_file, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n        browse_html = f.read()\n    \n    print(f\'Browse page HTML size: {len(browse_html):,} characters\')\n    \n    soup = BeautifulSoup(browse_html, \'html.parser\')\n    \n    # Get page title to understand what we\'re looking at\n    page_title = soup.find(\'title\')\n    if page_title:\n        print(f\'Page title: {page_title.get_text().strip()}\')\n    \n    # Look for any search results or artwork listings\n    print(\'\\n--- SEARCHING FOR ARTWORK CONTENT ---\')\n    \n    # Try to find any links that might lead to individual artworks\n    artwork_links = []\n    \n    for link in soup.find_all(\'a\', href=True):\n        href = link.get(\'href\')\n        text = link.get_text().strip()\n        \n        # Look for links that might be individual artworks\n        if ((\'/artwork/\' in href or \'/object/\' in href) and \n            len(text) > 5 and text not in [\'View\', \'More\', \'Learn More\']):\n            \n            full_url = urljoin(\'https://americanart.si.edu\', href)\n            artwork_links.append({\n                \'title\': text,\n                \'url\': full_url,\n                \'href\': href\n            })\n    \n    print(f\'Found {len(artwork_links)} potential artwork links\')\n    \n    if artwork_links:\n        print(\'\\nFirst 10 artwork links found:\')\n        for i, link in enumerate(artwork_links[:10], 1):\n            print(f\'{i:2d}. "{link["title"]}"\')\n            print(f\'    URL: {link["url"]}\')\n    \n    # Look for any JavaScript data or API endpoints that might contain artwork data\n    print(\'\\n--- LOOKING FOR JAVASCRIPT DATA ---\')\n    \n    scripts = soup.find_all(\'script\')\n    print(f\'Found {len(scripts)} script tags\')\n    \n    # Look for JSON data in scripts\n    json_data_found = []\n    \n    for i, script in enumerate(scripts):\n        script_content = script.get_text()\n        if script_content and len(script_content) > 100:\n            # Look for JSON-like structures\n            if (\'{\' in script_content and \'}\' in script_content and \n                (\'artwork\' in script_content.lower() or \'title\' in script_content.lower())):\n                \n                print(f\'Script {i+1} contains potential artwork data ({len(script_content):,} chars)\')\n                \n                # Try to extract JSON objects\n                json_matches = re.findall(r\'\\{[^{}]*"[^"]*"[^{}]*\\}\', script_content)\n                if json_matches:\n                    print(f\'  Found {len(json_matches)} potential JSON objects\')\n                    json_data_found.extend(json_matches[:5])  # Keep first 5\n    \n    if json_data_found:\n        print(\'\\nSample JSON data found:\')\n        for i, json_str in enumerate(json_data_found[:3], 1):\n            print(f\'{i}. {json_str[:100]}...\')\n    \n    # Look for any form elements that might help with pagination or search\n    print(\'\\n--- ANALYZING PAGE STRUCTURE ---\')\n    \n    forms = soup.find_all(\'form\')\n    print(f\'Found {len(forms)} forms\')\n    \n    for i, form in enumerate(forms, 1):\n        action = form.get(\'action\', \'No action\')\n        method = form.get(\'method\', \'GET\')\n        inputs = form.find_all(\'input\')\n        \n        print(f\'Form {i}: {action} ({method}) - {len(inputs)} inputs\')\n        \n        for inp in inputs:\n            name = inp.get(\'name\', \'unnamed\')\n            input_type = inp.get(\'type\', \'text\')\n            value = inp.get(\'value\', \'\')\n            print(f\'  - {name} ({input_type}): "{value}"\')\n    \n    # Look for pagination or load more functionality\n    pagination_elements = soup.find_all([\'nav\', \'div\', \'button\'], \n                                       class_=re.compile(r\'pag|load|more|next|prev\', re.I))\n    \n    if pagination_elements:\n        print(f\'\\nFound {len(pagination_elements)} pagination/load elements:\')\n        for elem in pagination_elements[:5]:\n            classes = elem.get(\'class\', [])\n            text = elem.get_text().strip()[:50]\n            print(f\'  - {elem.name}: classes={classes}, text="{text}..."\')\n    \n    # Try to understand if this is a search results page or a landing page\n    page_text = soup.get_text().lower()\n    \n    if \'no results\' in page_text or \'no artworks found\' in page_text:\n        print(\'\\n⚠ Page indicates no results found\')\n    elif \'search for\' in page_text and \'enter\' in page_text:\n        print(\'\\n⚠ Page appears to be a search form rather than results\')\n    elif len(artwork_links) == 0 and \'browse\' in page_text:\n        print(\'\\n⚠ Page appears to be a browse landing page without specific artworks\')\n    \nelse:\n    print(\'❌ Browse artworks HTML file not found\')\n\nprint(\'\\n=== TRYING DIRECT API OR AJAX APPROACH ===\\n\')\n\n# Based on the analysis, try to find the actual API endpoint\n# Many modern museum sites use AJAX to load artwork data\n\napi_endpoints_to_try = [\n    \'https://americanart.si.edu/api/search/artworks\',\n    \'https://americanart.si.edu/search/artworks.json\',\n    \'https://americanart.si.edu/api/artworks\',\n    \'https://americanart.si.edu/collections/api/search\'\n]\n\nheaders = {\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/120.0.0.0 Safari/537.36\',\n    \'Accept\': \'application/json, text/html, */*\',\n    \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.9\',\n    \'X-Requested-With\': \'XMLHttpRequest\'  # Common AJAX header\n}\n\nfor i, endpoint in enumerate(api_endpoints_to_try, 1):\n    print(f\'--- Trying API endpoint {i}: {endpoint} ---\')\n    \n    try:\n        response = requests.get(endpoint, headers=headers, timeout=20)\n        print(f\'Response status: {response.status_code}\')\n        print(f\'Content type: {response.headers.get("content-type", "unknown")}\')\n        print(f\'Content length: {len(response.content):,} bytes\')\n        \n        if response.status_code == 200:\n            content_type = response.headers.get(\'content-type\', \'\').lower()\n            \n            if \'json\' in content_type:\n                print(\'✓ JSON response received!\')\n                try:\n                    data = response.json()\n                    print(f\'JSON structure: {type(data)}\')\n                    \n                    if isinstance(data, dict):\n                        print(f\'JSON keys: {list(data.keys())}\')\n                        \n                        # Look for artwork data\n                        for key in [\'artworks\', \'results\', \'items\', \'data\', \'objects\']:\n                            if key in data:\n                                artworks = data[key]\n                                print(f\'Found {len(artworks) if isinstance(artworks, list) else "unknown"} items under "{key}"\')\n                                \n                                if isinstance(artworks, list) and len(artworks) > 0:\n                                    sample = artworks[0]\n                                    print(f\'Sample artwork keys: {list(sample.keys()) if isinstance(sample, dict) else "not a dict"}\')\n                                    break\n                    \n                    # Save the JSON response\n                    json_file = f\'workspace/smithsonian_api_response_{i}.json\'\n                    with open(json_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                        json.dump(data, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)\n                    print(f\'✓ JSON response saved to: {json_file}\')\n                    \n                except json.JSONDecodeError as e:\n                    print(f\'❌ JSON decode error: {str(e)}\')\n            \n            elif \'html\' in content_type:\n                print(\'HTML response received\')\n                # Check if it\'s different from what we already have\n                if len(response.text) > 50000:  # Substantial content\n                    html_file = f\'workspace/smithsonian_api_html_response_{i}.html\'\n                    with open(html_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                        f.write(response.text)\n                    print(f\'✓ HTML response saved to: {html_file}\')\n        \n        elif response.status_code == 404:\n            print(\'Endpoint not found\')\n        else:\n            print(f\'Unexpected status code: {response.status_code}\')\n        \n        time.sleep(1)  # Rate limiting\n        \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\'Error accessing endpoint: {str(e)}\')\n\nprint(\'\\n=== TRYING SEARCH WITH SPECIFIC LITERARY TERMS ===\\n\')\n\n# Try searching for specific terms that might indicate literary quotations\nliterary_search_terms = [\n    \'chapter\',\n    \'verse\',\n    \'canto\',\n    \'poem\',\n    \'novel\',\n    \'book\',\n    \'quotation\',\n    \'literary\'\n]\n\nsearch_results = []\n\nfor i, term in enumerate(literary_search_terms[:3], 1):  # Try first 3 terms\n    print(f\'--- Literary Search {i}: "{term}" ---\')\n    \n    # Try the search URL that seemed to work in the previous attempt\n    search_url = f\'https://americanart.si.edu/search/artworks?q={quote(term)}\'\n    \n    try:\n        response = requests.get(search_url, headers=headers, timeout=20)\n        print(f\'Search response status: {response.status_code}\')\n        \n        if response.status_code == 200:\n            search_soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, \'html.parser\')\n            \n            # Look for actual artwork results\n            # Try multiple selectors that might contain artwork information\n            result_selectors = [\n                \'.search-result\',\n                \'.artwork-result\', \n                \'.result-item\',\n                \'.artwork-item\',\n                \'.collection-item\',\n                \'article\',\n                \'.card\',\n                \'[data-artwork]\',\n                \'.item\'\n            ]\n            \n            found_results = []\n            \n            for selector in result_selectors:\n                results = search_soup.select(selector)\n                if results and len(results) > 3:  # Only consider substantial result sets\n                    print(f\'  Found {len(results)} results using selector: {selector}\')\n                    found_results = results\n                    break\n            \n            if found_results:\n                print(f\'  Analyzing first 5 results:\')\n                \n                for j, result in enumerate(found_results[:5], 1):\n                    # Extract title and link\n                    title_elem = result.find([\'h1\', \'h2\', \'h3\', \'h4\', \'h5\', \'a\'])\n                    title = title_elem.get_text().strip() if title_elem else \'No title found\'\n                    \n                    link_elem = result.find(\'a\', href=True)\n                    link_url = urljoin(\'https://americanart.si.edu\', link_elem.get(\'href\')) if link_elem else None\n                    \n                    print(f\'    {j}. "{title[:60]}..."\')\n                    if link_url:\n                        print(f\'       URL: {link_url}\')\n                    \n                    # Check if this looks like a literary quotation\n                    title_lower = title.lower()\n                    literary_indicators = [\n                        \'chapter\', \'book\', \'canto\', \'verse\', \'stanza\', \'act\', \'scene\',\n                        \'from\', \'after\', \'part\', \'volume\', \'line\', \'page\'\n                    ]\n                    \n                    indicators_found = [ind for ind in literary_indicators if ind in title_lower]\n                    \n                    if indicators_found:\n                        print(f\'       *** LITERARY INDICATORS: {indicators_found} ***\')\n                        \n                        search_results.append({\n                            \'title\': title,\n                            \'url\': link_url,\n                            \'search_term\': term,\n                            \'literary_indicators\': indicators_found\n                        })\n            \n            else:\n                print(f\'  No substantial results found for "{term}"\')\n                \n                # Check if we got the generic page again\n                page_text = search_soup.get_text().lower()\n                if \'explore the art\' in page_text and len(page_text) < 2000:\n                    print(f\'  → Received generic "Explore the Art" page\')\n        \n        time.sleep(2)  # Rate limiting\n        \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\'  Error searching for "{term}": {str(e)}\')\n\nprint(\'\\n=== COMPREHENSIVE SEARCH SUMMARY ===\\n\')\n\nif search_results:\n    print(f\'✓ Found {len(search_results)} artworks with literary indicators:\')\n    \n    for i, result in enumerate(search_results, 1):\n        print(f\'\\n{i}. "{result["title"]}"\')\n        print(f\'   Search term: {result["search_term"]}\')\n        print(f\'   Literary indicators: {result["literary_indicators"]}\')\n        if result.get(\'url\'):\n            print(f\'   URL: {result["url"]}\')\n    \n    # Look for potential series (titles that might be from the same literary work)\n    print(\'\\n--- ANALYZING FOR POTENTIAL SERIES ---\')\n    \n    # Group by common words in titles\n    title_groups = {}\n    \n    for result in search_results:\n        title = result[\'title\']\n        # Extract significant words (capitalized, longer than 3 chars)\n        words = re.findall(r\'\\b[A-Z][a-z]{3,}\\b\', title)\n        \n        if words:\n            # Use first 2-3 significant words as grouping key\n            group_key = \' \'.join(words[:3]).lower()\n            \n            if group_key not in title_groups:\n                title_groups[group_key] = []\n            title_groups[group_key].append(result)\n    \n    # Find groups with multiple titles\n    series_groups = {k: v for k, v in title_groups.items() if len(v) >= 2}\n    \n    if series_groups:\n        print(f\'Found {len(series_groups)} potential title series:\')\n        \n        for group_key, group_items in series_groups.items():\n            print(f\'\\n*** SERIES: "{group_key}" ({len(group_items)} titles) ***\')\n            for item in group_items:\n                print(f\'  - {item["title"]}\')\n            print(f\'  → These may be quotes from the same literary work\')\n    \n    # Save comprehensive results\n    final_results = {\n        \'search_timestamp\': time.strftime(\'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S\'),\n        \'objective\': \'Find paintings with titles that appear to be quotes from the same literary work\',\n        \'methodology\': \'Searched Smithsonian American Art Museum collection for literary quotation patterns\',\n        \'total_literary_artworks_found\': len(search_results),\n        \'literary_artworks\': search_results,\n        \'potential_series\': series_groups,\n        \'search_terms_used\': literary_search_terms[:3]\n    }\n    \n    with open(\'workspace/smithsonian_literary_quotations_final.json\', \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n        json.dump(final_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)\n    \n    print(f\'\\n✓ Final results saved to: workspace/smithsonian_literary_quotations_final.json\')\n    \n    print(\'\\n🎯 SUCCESS: Found artworks with literary quotation patterns!\')\n    print(\'Next steps:\')\n    print(\'1. Access individual artwork pages to get creation dates\')\n    print(\'2. Filter for works created by August 2023 or earlier\')\n    print(\'3. Analyze artist statements and descriptions for source identification\')\n    print(\'4. Focus on any series that might reference the same literary work\')\n    \nelse:\n    print(\'⚠ No artworks with clear literary quotation patterns found\')\n    print(\'\\nThis could indicate:\')\n    print(\'1. The search interface requires different parameters\')\n    print(\'2. Literary quotation titles use different naming conventions\')\n    print(\'3. The collection may need to be browsed by specific artists or time periods\')\n    print(\'4. The paintings may be in a special collection or exhibition\')\n\nprint(\'\\nObjective: Identify paintings with titles that appear to be quotes from the same literary work\')\nif search_results:\n    print(\'Status: Literary quotation patterns identified - ready for detailed analysis\')\nelse:\n    print(\'Status: Search methodology needs refinement for this specific collection\')',
