    "code": 'import os\nimport json\nfrom bs4 import BeautifulSoup\nimport requests\nfrom urllib.parse import urljoin, quote\nimport time\nimport re\n\nprint(\'=== DEEP ANALYSIS OF SMITHSONIAN SEARCH RESULTS AND ARTWORK EXTRACTION ===\')\nprint(\'Objective: Extract actual artwork data from Smithsonian search responses and identify literary quotations\\n\')\n\n# First, let\'s inspect the structure of files we have to understand what data is available\nprint(\'=== INSPECTING WORKSPACE FILES STRUCTURE ===\')\nworkspace_files = [f for f in os.listdir(\'workspace\') if os.path.isfile(os.path.join(\'workspace\', f))]\nprint(f\'Total files in workspace: {len(workspace_files)}\')\n\n# Focus on Smithsonian-related files\nsmithsonian_files = [f for f in workspace_files if \'smithsonian\' in f.lower()]\nprint(f\'\\nSmithsonian-related files: {len(smithsonian_files)}\')\nfor file in smithsonian_files:\n    file_path = os.path.join(\'workspace\', file)\n    file_size = os.path.getsize(file_path)\n    print(f\'  - {file}: {file_size:,} bytes\')\n\n# Let\'s examine the browse artworks HTML file more carefully\nbrowse_file = \'workspace/smithsonian_browse_artworks.html\'\n\nif os.path.exists(browse_file):\n    print(f\'\\n=== DETAILED ANALYSIS OF BROWSE ARTWORKS PAGE ===\')\n    \n    with open(browse_file, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n        browse_html = f.read()\n    \n    print(f\'File size: {len(browse_html):,} characters\')\n    \n    soup = BeautifulSoup(browse_html, \'html.parser\')\n    \n    # Extract and analyze the page title and main content\n    page_title = soup.find(\'title\')\n    print(f\'Page title: {page_title.get_text().strip() if page_title else "No title"}\')\n    \n    # Look for any search interface elements\n    print(\'\\n--- ANALYZING SEARCH INTERFACE ELEMENTS ---\')\n    \n    # Find search forms and their structure\n    search_forms = soup.find_all(\'form\')\n    print(f\'Found {len(search_forms)} forms\')\n    \n    for i, form in enumerate(search_forms, 1):\n        action = form.get(\'action\', \'No action\')\n        method = form.get(\'method\', \'GET\')\n        print(f\'\\nForm {i}: Action="{action}" Method="{method}"\')\n        \n        # Analyze form inputs\n        inputs = form.find_all(\'input\')\n        selects = form.find_all(\'select\')\n        \n        for inp in inputs:\n            name = inp.get(\'name\', \'unnamed\')\n            input_type = inp.get(\'type\', \'text\')\n            placeholder = inp.get(\'placeholder\', \'\')\n            value = inp.get(\'value\', \'\')\n            print(f\'  Input: {name} ({input_type}) placeholder="{placeholder}" value="{value}"\')\n        \n        for sel in selects:\n            name = sel.get(\'name\', \'unnamed\')\n            options = sel.find_all(\'option\')\n            print(f\'  Select: {name} with {len(options)} options\')\n            for opt in options[:3]:  # Show first 3 options\n                print(f\'    - {opt.get("value", "")} : {opt.get_text().strip()}\')\n    \n    # Look for any existing search results or artwork listings\n    print(\'\\n--- SEARCHING FOR ARTWORK CONTENT PATTERNS ---\')\n    \n    # Try various selectors that museums commonly use\n    artwork_selectors = [\n        \'article\',\n        \'.artwork\',\n        \'.collection-item\', \n        \'.search-result\',\n        \'.result\',\n        \'.item\',\n        \'.card\',\n        \'.object\',\n        \'[data-artwork]\',\n        \'[data-object]\',\n        \'.artwork-card\',\n        \'.collection-object\',\n        \'.museum-object\'\n    ]\n    \n    potential_artworks = []\n    \n    for selector in artwork_selectors:\n        elements = soup.select(selector)\n        if elements:\n            print(f\'Selector "{selector}": {len(elements)} elements found\')\n            \n            # Analyze first few elements to see if they contain artwork data\n            for i, elem in enumerate(elements[:3], 1):\n                text_content = elem.get_text().strip()[:100]\n                links = elem.find_all(\'a\', href=True)\n                images = elem.find_all(\'img\')\n                \n                print(f\'  Element {i}: {len(text_content)} chars, {len(links)} links, {len(images)} images\')\n                print(f\'    Text preview: "{text_content}..."\')\n                \n                # Check if this looks like artwork content\n                if links and (len(text_content) > 20 or images):\n                    for link in links:\n                        href = link.get(\'href\')\n                        link_text = link.get_text().strip()\n                        if href and len(link_text) > 5:\n                            potential_artworks.append({\n                                \'title\': link_text,\n                                \'url\': urljoin(\'https://americanart.si.edu\', href),\n                                \'selector\': selector,\n                                \'element_index\': i\n                            })\n    \n    if potential_artworks:\n        print(f\'\\n*** FOUND {len(potential_artworks)} POTENTIAL ARTWORKS ***\')\n        for i, artwork in enumerate(potential_artworks[:10], 1):\n            print(f\'{i:2d}. "{artwork["title"]}"\')\n            print(f\'    URL: {artwork["url"]}\')\n            print(f\'    Found via: {artwork["selector"]}\')\n    else:\n        print(\'\\n⚠ No potential artwork content found using standard selectors\')\n    \n    # Look for JavaScript or AJAX loading mechanisms\n    print(\'\\n--- ANALYZING JAVASCRIPT AND AJAX MECHANISMS ---\')\n    \n    scripts = soup.find_all(\'script\')\n    print(f\'Found {len(scripts)} script tags\')\n    \n    ajax_indicators = []\n    \n    for i, script in enumerate(scripts):\n        script_content = script.get_text() if script.get_text() else \'\'\n        \n        if len(script_content) > 100:\n            # Look for AJAX/API indicators\n            ajax_patterns = [\n                r\'ajax\',\n                r\'fetch\\(\',\n                r\'XMLHttpRequest\',\n                r\'\\.json\\(\',\n                r\'api/\',\n                r\'search/\',\n                r\'artworks\',\n                r\'collection\'\n            ]\n            \n            found_patterns = []\n            for pattern in ajax_patterns:\n                if re.search(pattern, script_content, re.IGNORECASE):\n                    found_patterns.append(pattern)\n            \n            if found_patterns:\n                print(f\'Script {i+1} ({len(script_content):,} chars) contains: {found_patterns}\')\n                ajax_indicators.append({\n                    \'script_index\': i+1,\n                    \'content_length\': len(script_content),\n                    \'patterns\': found_patterns,\n                    \'preview\': script_content[:200].replace(\'\\n\', \' \')\n                })\n    \n    if ajax_indicators:\n        print(f\'\\nFound {len(ajax_indicators)} scripts with AJAX/API indicators:\')\n        for indicator in ajax_indicators[:3]:\n            print(f\'  Script {indicator["script_index"]}: {indicator["patterns"]}\')\n            print(f\'    Preview: "{indicator["preview"]}..."\')\n    \n    # Try to find any data attributes or configuration that might reveal API endpoints\n    print(\'\\n--- LOOKING FOR DATA ATTRIBUTES AND CONFIGURATION ---\')\n    \n    data_elements = soup.find_all(attrs=lambda x: x and any(k.startswith(\'data-\') for k in x.keys()))\n    print(f\'Found {len(data_elements)} elements with data attributes\')\n    \n    relevant_data = []\n    for elem in data_elements:\n        for attr, value in elem.attrs.items():\n            if attr.startswith(\'data-\') and (\'url\' in attr or \'api\' in attr or \'search\' in attr):\n                relevant_data.append({\n                    \'element\': elem.name,\n                    \'attribute\': attr,\n                    \'value\': value\n                })\n    \n    if relevant_data:\n        print(\'Relevant data attributes found:\')\n        for data in relevant_data[:5]:\n            print(f\'  {data["element"]} {data["attribute"]}="{data["value"]}"\')\n\nprint(\'\\n=== TRYING ENHANCED SEARCH APPROACHES ===\')\n\n# Based on the analysis, try more targeted search approaches\nheaders = {\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/120.0.0.0 Safari/537.36\',\n    \'Accept\': \'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8\',\n    \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.9\',\n    \'Referer\': \'https://americanart.si.edu/collections/search\'\n}\n\n# Try different search approaches that might work better\nsearch_approaches = [\n    # Try searching with pagination parameters\n    \'https://americanart.si.edu/search/artworks?page=0\',\n    \'https://americanart.si.edu/search/artworks?page=1\',\n    # Try with specific content type\n    \'https://americanart.si.edu/search/artworks?content_type=artwork&page=0\',\n    # Try the search form action directly\n    \'https://americanart.si.edu/search?query=painting\',\n    \'https://americanart.si.edu/search?query=artwork\'\n]\n\nsearch_results_found = []\n\nfor i, search_url in enumerate(search_approaches[:3], 1):  # Try first 3 approaches\n    print(f\'\\n--- Enhanced Search Approach {i}: {search_url} ---\')\n    \n    try:\n        response = requests.get(search_url, headers=headers, timeout=30)\n        print(f\'Response status: {response.status_code}\')\n        print(f\'Content length: {len(response.content):,} bytes\')\n        \n        if response.status_code == 200:\n            # Save the response for analysis\n            response_file = f\'workspace/smithsonian_enhanced_search_{i}.html\'\n            with open(response_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                f.write(response.text)\n            print(f\'✓ Response saved to: {response_file}\')\n            \n            # Parse and analyze the response\n            search_soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, \'html.parser\')\n            \n            # Check if this is different from the generic browse page\n            page_text = search_soup.get_text()\n            \n            # Look for artwork-specific content\n            artwork_indicators = [\n                \'artist:\', \'title:\', \'date:\', \'medium:\', \'dimensions:\',\n                \'collection\', \'accession\', \'artwork\', \'painting\', \'sculpture\'\n            ]\n            \n            indicators_found = [ind for ind in artwork_indicators if ind.lower() in page_text.lower()]\n            \n            if indicators_found:\n                print(f\'  ✓ Artwork indicators found: {indicators_found[:5]}\')\n                \n                # Try to extract actual artwork information\n                # Look for structured data or repeated patterns\n                \n                # Method 1: Look for links to individual artwork pages\n                artwork_links = []\n                for link in search_soup.find_all(\'a\', href=True):\n                    href = link.get(\'href\')\n                    text = link.get_text().strip()\n                    \n                    # Check if this looks like an artwork link\n                    if ((\'/artwork/\' in href or \'/object/\' in href) and \n                        len(text) > 10 and \n                        not any(skip in text.lower() for skip in [\'view\', \'more\', \'learn\', \'browse\'])):\n                        \n                        artwork_links.append({\n                            \'title\': text,\n                            \'url\': urljoin(\'https://americanart.si.edu\', href),\n                            \'href\': href\n                        })\n                \n                if artwork_links:\n                    print(f\'  Found {len(artwork_links)} artwork links:\')\n                    \n                    for j, artwork in enumerate(artwork_links[:5], 1):\n                        print(f\'    {j}. "{artwork["title"]}"\')\n                        print(f\'       URL: {artwork["url"]}\')\n                        \n                        # Check for literary quotation patterns\n                        title_lower = artwork[\'title\'].lower()\n                        literary_patterns = [\n                            r\'chapter\\s+\\d+\',\n                            r\'book\\s+\\d+\', \n                            r\'canto\\s+\\d+\',\n                            r\'part\\s+[ivx]+\',\n                            r\'act\\s+[ivx]+\',\n                            r\'scene\\s+[ivx]+\',\n                            r\'verse\\s+\\d+\',\n                            r\'from\\s+["\\\']\',\n                            r\'after\\s+["\\\']\',\n                            r\'\\b[ivx]+\\.\',\n                            r\'\\b\\d+\\.\',\n                            r\'first|second|third|fourth|fifth\'\n                        ]\n                        \n                        matches = []\n                        for pattern in literary_patterns:\n                            if re.search(pattern, title_lower):\n                                matches.append(pattern)\n                        \n                        if matches:\n                            print(f\'       *** LITERARY QUOTATION PATTERNS: {matches} ***\')\n                            \n                            search_results_found.append({\n                                \'title\': artwork[\'title\'],\n                                \'url\': artwork[\'url\'],\n                                \'literary_patterns\': matches,\n                                \'search_approach\': i,\n                                \'search_url\': search_url\n                            })\n                \n                # Method 2: Look for structured data in the page\n                # Sometimes museums embed JSON-LD or other structured data\n                json_ld_scripts = search_soup.find_all(\'script\', type=\'application/ld+json\')\n                if json_ld_scripts:\n                    print(f\'  Found {len(json_ld_scripts)} JSON-LD scripts\')\n                    \n                    for j, script in enumerate(json_ld_scripts, 1):\n                        try:\n                            data = json.loads(script.get_text())\n                            print(f\'    JSON-LD {j}: {type(data)} with keys: {list(data.keys()) if isinstance(data, dict) else "not a dict"}\')\n                        except json.JSONDecodeError:\n                            print(f\'    JSON-LD {j}: Invalid JSON\')\n            \n            else:\n                print(f\'  No artwork indicators found - may be generic page\')\n                \n                # Check if it\'s the same generic content\n                if \'explore the art\' in page_text.lower() and len(page_text) < 3000:\n                    print(f\'  → Generic "Explore the Art" page returned\')\n        \n        time.sleep(2)  # Rate limiting\n        \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\'  Error with search approach {i}: {str(e)}\')\n\nprint(\'\\n=== COMPREHENSIVE RESULTS SUMMARY ===\')\n\nif search_results_found:\n    print(f\'\\n🎯 SUCCESS: Found {len(search_results_found)} artworks with literary quotation patterns!\')\n    \n    for i, result in enumerate(search_results_found, 1):\n        print(f\'\\n{i}. "{result["title"]}"\')\n        print(f\'   URL: {result["url"]}\')\n        print(f\'   Literary patterns: {result["literary_patterns"]}\')\n        print(f\'   Found via search approach: {result["search_approach"]}\')\n    \n    # Group results to find potential series from the same literary work\n    print(\'\\n--- ANALYZING FOR LITERARY SERIES ---\')\n    \n    # Extract key words from titles to group them\n    title_groups = {}\n    \n    for result in search_results_found:\n        title = result[\'title\']\n        # Extract significant words (capitalized, 3+ characters)\n        words = re.findall(r\'\\b[A-Z][a-z]{2,}\\b\', title)\n        \n        if words:\n            # Create grouping key from first few significant words\n            group_key = \' \'.join(words[:3]).lower()\n            \n            if group_key not in title_groups:\n                title_groups[group_key] = []\n            title_groups[group_key].append(result)\n    \n    # Find groups with multiple titles (potential series)\n    series_groups = {k: v for k, v in title_groups.items() if len(v) >= 2}\n    \n    if series_groups:\n        print(f\'Found {len(series_groups)} potential literary series:\')\n        \n        for group_key, group_items in series_groups.items():\n            print(f\'\\n*** SERIES: "{group_key}" ({len(group_items)} artworks) ***\')\n            for item in group_items:\n                print(f\'  - {item["title"]}\')\n            print(f\'  → These artworks may quote from the same literary work\')\n            print(f\'  → This could be the literary work referenced in Federico Lauria\\\'s footnote 397\')\n    \n    # Save comprehensive results\n    final_results = {\n        \'search_timestamp\': time.strftime(\'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S\'),\n        \'objective\': \'Find paintings with titles that appear to be quotes from the same literary work (alternative approach to accessing Federico Lauria footnote 397)\',\n        \'methodology\': \'Enhanced search of Smithsonian American Art Museum collection with literary quotation pattern analysis\',\n        \'total_literary_artworks_found\': len(search_results_found),\n        \'literary_artworks\': search_results_found,\n        \'potential_series\': series_groups,\n        \'success\': True if search_results_found else False,\n        \'next_steps\': [\n            \'Access individual artwork pages to verify creation dates (August 2023 or earlier)\',\n            \'Examine artist statements and descriptions for literary source identification\',\n            \'Focus on series with multiple related titles\',\n            \'Research the identified literary work to understand its connection to Federico Lauria\\\'s research\'\n        ]\n    }\n    \n    with open(\'workspace/smithsonian_literary_quotations_success.json\', \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n        json.dump(final_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)\n    \n    print(f\'\\n✓ Success results saved to: workspace/smithsonian_literary_quotations_success.json\')\n    \n    print(\'\\n🎯 MISSION ACCOMPLISHED!\')\n    print(\'Alternative approach successful: Found paintings with literary quotation titles\')\n    print(\'This reverse-engineering method has identified potential artworks that may be\')\n    print(\'referenced in Federico Lauria\\\'s footnote 397 without needing direct dissertation access.\')\n    \nelse:\n    print(\'\\n⚠ No clear literary quotation patterns found in current search results\')\n    \n    # Collect search endpoints\n        if action and action not in [\'No action\', \'#\']:\n            if action.startswith(\'/\'):\n                full_action = f\'https://americanart.si.edu{action}\'\n            else:\n                full_action = action\n            search_endpoints.append(full_action)\n        \n        # Analyze form inputs\n        inputs = form.find_all(\'input\')\n        for inp in inputs:\n            name = inp.get(\'name\', \'unnamed\')\n            input_type = inp.get(\'type\', \'text\')\n            placeholder = inp.get(\'placeholder\', \'\')\n            print(f\'  Input: {name} ({input_type}) placeholder="{placeholder}"\')\n    \n    print(f\'\\nIdentified search endpoints: {search_endpoints}\')\n    \n    # Look for JavaScript data with AJAX indicators (fixed approach)\n    print(\'\\n--- JAVASCRIPT ANALYSIS ---\')\n    scripts = soup.find_all(\'script\')\n    print(f\'Found {len(scripts)} script tags\')\n    \n    ajax_data = []\n    \n    for i, script in enumerate(scripts):\n        script_content = script.get_text() if script.get_text() else \'\'\n        \n        if len(script_content) > 100:\n            # Look for AJAX/API indicators\n            ajax_patterns = [\n                \'ajax\', \'fetch(\', \'XMLHttpRequest\', \'.json(\', \n                \'api/\', \'search/\', \'artworks\', \'collection\'\n            ]\n            \n            found_patterns = []\n            for pattern in ajax_patterns:\n                if pattern.lower() in script_content.lower():\n                    found_patterns.append(pattern)\n            \n            if found_patterns:\n                print(f\'Script {i+1} ({len(script_content):,} chars) contains: {found_patterns}\')\n                ajax_data.append({\n                    \'script_index\': i+1,\n                    \'content_length\': len(script_content),\n                    \'patterns\': found_patterns,\n                    \'preview\': script_content[:300].replace(\'\\n\', \' \')\n                })\n    \n    if ajax_data:\n        print(f\'\\nFound {len(ajax_data)} scripts with AJAX/API indicators:\')\n        for data in ajax_data[:2]:  # Show first 2\n            print(f\'  Script {data["script_index"]}: {data["patterns"]}\')\n            print(f\'    Preview: "{data["preview"]}..."\')\n    \n    # Fixed data attributes search - handle both dict and string attributes\n    print(\'\\n--- DATA ATTRIBUTES ANALYSIS (FIXED) ---\')\n    \n    data_elements = []\n    for elem in soup.find_all():\n        if hasattr(elem, \'attrs\') and elem.attrs:\n            for attr, value in elem.attrs.items():\n                if attr.startswith(\'data-\') and (\'url\' in attr or \'api\' in attr or \'search\' in attr):\n                    data_elements.append({\n                        \'element\': elem.name,\n                        \'attribute\': attr,\n                        \'value\': str(value)  # Convert to string to handle both list and string values\n                    })\n    \n    if data_elements:\n        print(f\'Found {len(data_elements)} relevant data attributes:\')\n        for data in data_elements[:5]:\n            print(f\'  {data["element"]} {data["attribute"]}="{data["value"]}"\')\n    else:\n        print(\'No relevant data attributes found\')\n\nprint(\'\\n=== TRYING DIRECT SEARCH WITH LITERARY TERMS ===\')\n\n# Try searching for specific literary terms using the identified search endpoints\nheaders = {\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/120.0.0.0 Safari/537.36\',\n    \'Accept\': \'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8\',\n    \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.9\',\n    \'Referer\': \'https://americanart.si.edu/collections/search\'\n}\n\n# Literary terms that might indicate quotation titles\nliterary_search_terms = [\n    \'chapter\',\n    \'verse\', \n    \'canto\',\n    \'book\',\n    \'poem\',\n    \'novel\',\n    \'quotation\',\n    \'literary\',\n    \'from\',\n    \'after\'\n]\n\nsearch_results = []\n\n# Try different search URL patterns\nsearch_patterns = [\n    \'https://americanart.si.edu/search?query={}\',\n    \'https://americanart.si.edu/search/artworks?q={}\',\n    \'https://americanart.si.edu/collections/search?q={}\'\n]\n\nfor i, term in enumerate(literary_search_terms[:5], 1):  # Try first 5 terms\n    print(f\'\\n--- Literary Search {i}: "{term}" ---\')\n    \n    for j, pattern in enumerate(search_patterns, 1):\n        search_url = pattern.format(quote(term))\n        print(f\'  Pattern {j}: {search_url}\')\n        \n        try:\n            response = requests.get(search_url, headers=headers, timeout=20)\n            print(f\'  Response status: {response.status_code}\')\n            print(f\'  Content length: {len(response.content):,} bytes\')\n            \n            if response.status_code == 200:\n                # Save response for analysis\n                response_file = f\'workspace/smithsonian_search_{term}_{j}.html\'\n                with open(response_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                    f.write(response.text)\n                print(f\'  ✓ Response saved to: {response_file}\')\n                \n                # Parse and analyze the response\n                search_soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, \'html.parser\')\n                page_text = search_soup.get_text().lower()\n                \n                # Check if this is different from generic browse page\n                if \'explore the art\' in page_text and \'browse artwork\' in page_text and len(page_text) < 3000:\n                    print(f\'  → Generic browse page returned\')\n                else:\n                    print(f\'  → Different content returned ({len(page_text):,} chars)\')\n                    \n                    # Look for artwork links\n                    artwork_links = []\n                    for link in search_soup.find_all(\'a\', href=True):\n                        href = link.get(\'href\')\n                        text = link.get_text().strip()\n                        \n                        # Check if this looks like an artwork link\n                        if ((\'/artwork/\' in href or \'/object/\' in href) and \n                            len(text) > 10 and \n                            not any(skip in text.lower() for skip in [\'view\', \'more\', \'learn\', \'browse\', \'explore\'])):\n                            \n                            artwork_links.append({\n                                \'title\': text,\n                                \'url\': urljoin(\'https://americanart.si.edu\', href),\n                                \'search_term\': term,\n                                \'search_pattern\': j\n                            })\n                    \n                    if artwork_links:\n                        print(f\'  ✓ Found {len(artwork_links)} artwork links!\')\n                        \n                        for k, artwork in enumerate(artwork_links[:3], 1):\n                            print(f\'    {k}. "{artwork["title"]}"\')\n                            print(f\'       URL: {artwork["url"]}"\')\n                            \n                            # Check for literary quotation patterns\n                            title_lower = artwork[\'title\'].lower()\n                            literary_patterns = [\n                                r\'chapter\\s+\\d+\',\n                                r\'book\\s+\\d+\', \n                                r\'canto\\s+\\d+\',\n                                r\'part\\s+[ivx]+\',\n                                r\'act\\s+[ivx]+\',\n                                r\'scene\\s+[ivx]+\',\n                                r\'verse\\s+\\d+\',\n                                r\'from\\s+["\\\']\',\n                                r\'after\\s+["\\\']\',\n                                r\'\\\\b[ivx]+\\\\.\',\n                                r\'\\\\b\\d+\\\\.\',\n                                r\'first|second|third|fourth|fifth\'\n                            ]\n                            \n                            pattern_matches = []\n                            for pattern in literary_patterns:\n                                if re.search(pattern, title_lower):\n                                    pattern_matches.append(pattern)\n                            \n                            if pattern_matches:\n                                print(f\'       *** LITERARY QUOTATION PATTERNS: {pattern_matches} ***\')\n                                \n                                search_results.append({\n                                    \'title\': artwork[\'title\'],\n                                    \'url\': artwork[\'url\'],\n                                    \'search_term\': term,\n                                    \'literary_patterns\': pattern_matches,\n                                    \'search_pattern_used\': j\n                                })\n                        \n                        # If we found results with this pattern, use it for remaining searches\n                        if artwork_links:\n                            print(f\'  → Pattern {j} successful, using for remaining searches\')\n                            break\n            \n            time.sleep(1)  # Parse the artwork page\n        soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, \'html.parser\')\n        \n        # Extract key artwork information\n        print(\'\\n=== EXTRACTING ARTWORK DETAILS ===\')\n        \n        # Get page title\n        page_title = soup.find(\'title\')\n        if page_title:\n            print(f\'Page title: {page_title.get_text().strip()}\')\n        \n        # Look for artwork title\n        title_selectors = [\'h1\', \'.artwork-title\', \'.title\', \'.object-title\']\n        artwork_title = None\n        for selector in title_selectors:\n            title_elem = soup.select_one(selector)\n            if title_elem:\n                title_text = title_elem.get_text().strip()\n                if len(title_text) > 3 and \'untitled\' in title_text.lower():\n                    artwork_title = title_text\n                    print(f\'Artwork title: {title_text}\')\n                    break\n        \n        # Look for artist information\n        artist_selectors = [\'.artist\', \'.creator\', \'.artist-name\', \'[data-artist]\']\n        artist_name = None\n        for selector in artist_selectors:\n            artist_elem = soup.select_one(selector)\n            if artist_elem:\n                artist_text = artist_elem.get_text().strip()\n                if len(artist_text) > 2:\n                    artist_name = artist_text\n                    print(f\'Artist: {artist_text}\')\n                    break\n        \n        # Look for creation date - this is critical for our August 2023 requirement\n        date_selectors = [\'.date\', \'.year\', \'.created\', \'.artwork-date\', \'[data-date]\']\n        creation_date = None\n        for selector in date_selectors:\n            date_elem = soup.select_one(selector)\n            if date_elem:\n                date_text = date_elem.get_text().strip()\n                # Look for year patterns\n                year_match = re.search(r\'\\b(19|20)\\d{2}\\b\', date_text)\n                if year_match:\n                    creation_date = date_text\n                    year = int(year_match.group())\n                    print(f\'Creation date: {date_text}\')\n                    \n                    # Check if it meets our August 2023 or earlier requirement\n                    if year <= 2023:\n                        print(f\'✓ Date verification: {year} is August 2023 or earlier\')\n                    else:\n                        print(f\'❌ Date verification: {year} is after August 2023\')\n                    break\n        \n        # Look for medium/materials\n        medium_selectors = [\'.medium\', \'.materials\', \'.artwork-medium\']\n        medium = None\n        for selector in medium_selectors:\n            medium_elem = soup.select_one(selector)\n            if medium_elem:\n                medium_text = medium_elem.get_text().strip()\n                if len(medium_text) > 3:\n                    medium = medium_text\n                    print(f\'Medium: {medium_text}\')\n                    break\n        \n        # Look for dimensions\n        dimension_selectors = [\'.dimensions\', \'.size\', \'.artwork-dimensions\']\n        dimensions = None\n        for selector in dimension_selectors:\n            dim_elem = soup.select_one(selector)\n            if dim_elem:\n                dim_text = dim_elem.get_text().strip()\n                if len(dim_text) > 3:\n                    dimensions = dim_text\n                    print(f\'Dimensions: {dim_text}\')\n                    break\n        \n        # Look for description or artist statement - this is key for literary source identification\n        print(\'\\n=== SEARCHING FOR LITERARY SOURCE INFORMATION ===\')\n        \n        description_selectors = [\n            \'.description\', \'.artwork-description\', \'.object-description\',\n            \'.artist-statement\', \'.statement\', \'.about\', \'.text\',\n            \'.content\', \'.body\', \'.details\'\n        ]\n        \n        descriptions_found = []\n        \n        for selector in description_selectors:\n            desc_elems = soup.select(selector)\n            for elem in desc_elems:\n                desc_text = elem.get_text().strip()\n                if len(desc_text) > 50:  # Substantial content\n                    descriptions_found.append({\n                        \'selector\': selector,\n                        \'text\': desc_text,\n                        \'length\': len(desc_text)\n                    })\n        \n        if descriptions_found:\n            print(f\'Found {len(descriptions_found)} description sections:\')\n            \n            for i, desc in enumerate(descriptions_found, 1):\n                print(f\'\\n--- Description {i} (via {desc["selector"]}) ---\')\n                print(f\'Length: {desc["length"]:,} characters\')\n                \n                # Show first 500 characters\n                preview = desc[\'text\'][:500]\n                print(f\'Preview: {preview}...\')\n                \n                # Look for literary indicators in the description\n                desc_lower = desc[\'text\'].lower()\n                literary_terms = [\n                    \'poem\', \'poetry\', \'poet\', \'verse\', \'stanza\',\n                    \'novel\', \'book\', \'chapter\', \'literature\', \'literary\',\n                    \'author\', \'writer\', \'text\', \'quotation\', \'quote\',\n                    \'inspired by\', \'based on\', \'from\', \'after\',\n                    \'series\', \'pond\', \'water\', \'reflection\'\n                ]\n                \n                found_terms = [term for term in literary_terms if term in desc_lower]\n                \n                if found_terms:\n                    print(f\'*** LITERARY TERMS FOUND: {found_terms} ***\')\n                    \n                    # Look for specific mentions of literary works or authors\n                    # Common patterns for literary references\n                    literary_patterns = [\n                        r\'inspired by ["\\\']([^"\\\'\\.]+)["\\\']\',\n                        r\'based on ["\\\']([^"\\\'\\.]+)["\\\']\',\n                        r\'from ["\\\']([^"\\\'\\.]+)["\\\']\',\n                        r\'after ["\\\']([^"\\\'\\.]+)["\\\']\',\n                        r\'by ([A-Z][a-z]+ [A-Z][a-z]+)\',  # Author names\n                        r\'the ([A-Z][a-z]+ [A-Z][a-z]+)\',  # Book titles\n                    ]\n                    \n                    for pattern in literary_patterns:\n                        matches = re.findall(pattern, desc[\'text\'], re.IGNORECASE)\n                        if matches:\n                            print(f\'Literary reference pattern found: {pattern}\')\n                            print(f\'Matches: {matches}\')\n        \n        else:\n            print(\'No substantial description sections found\')\n        \n        # Look for any metadata or structured data\n        print(\'\\n=== SEARCHING FOR METADATA AND STRUCTURED DATA ===\')\n        \n        # Look for JSON-LD structured data\n        json_ld_scripts = soup.find_all(\'script\', type=\'application/ld+json\')\n        if json_ld_scripts:\n            print(f\'Found {len(json_ld_scripts)} JSON-LD scripts\')\n            \n            for i, script in enumerate(json_ld_scripts, 1):\n                try:\n                    data = json.loads(script.get_text())\n                    print(f\'JSON-LD {i}: {type(data)}\')\n                    \n                    if isinstance(data, dict):\n                        print(f\'  Keys: {list(data.keys())}\')\n                        \n                        # Look for artwork-specific fields\n                        artwork_fields = [\'name\', \'title\', \'creator\', \'dateCreated\', \'description\', \'about\']\n                        for field in artwork_fields:\n                            if field in data:\n                                value = data[field]\n                                print(f\'  {field}: {str(value)[:100]}...\')\n                \n                except json.JSONDecodeError:\n                    print(f\'JSON-LD {i}: Invalid JSON\')\n        \n        # Look for meta tags with artwork information\n        meta_tags = soup.find_all(\'meta\')\n        relevant_meta = []\n        \n        for meta in meta_tags:\n            name = meta.get(\'name\', \'\')\n            property_attr = meta.get(\'property\', \'\')\n            content = meta.get(\'content\', \'\')\n            \n            if content and (name or property_attr):\n                # Look for artwork-related meta tags\n                if any(term in (name + property_attr).lower() for term in \n                      [\'title\', \'description\', \'artist\', \'creator\', \'date\', \'artwork\']):\n                    relevant_meta.append({\n                        \'name\': name,\n                        \'property\': property_attr,\n                        \'content\': content\n                    })\n        \n        if relevant_meta:\n            print(f\'\\nFound {len(relevant_meta)} relevant meta tags:\')\n            for meta in relevant_meta[:10]:  # Show first 10\n                identifier = meta[\'name\'] or meta[\'property\']\n                print(f\'  {identifier}: {meta["content"][:100]}...\')\n        \n        # Compile comprehensive artwork information\n        artwork_info = {\n            \'title\': artwork_title,\n            \'artist\': artist_name,\n            \'creation_date\': creation_date,\n            \'medium\': medium,\n            \'dimensions\': dimensions,\n            \'url\': artwork_url,\n            \'descriptions\': descriptions_found,\n            \'literary_indicators\': [\'from\'],  # From our previous analysis\n            \'meets_date_requirement\': creation_date and any(int(match.group()) <= 2023 \n                                                          for match in re.finditer(r\'\\b(19|20)\\d{2}\\b\', creation_date)),\n            \'analysis_timestamp\': time.strftime(\'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S\')\n        }\n        \n        # Save detailed artwork analysis\n        artwork_analysis_file = \'workspace/smithsonian_pond_series_artwork_analysis.json\'\n        with open(artwork_analysis_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n            json.dump(artwork_info, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)\n        \n        print(f\'\\n✓ Detailed artwork analysis saved to: {artwork_analysis_file}\')\n        \n        # Save the artist page\n            artist_page_file = f\'workspace/smithsonian_artist_gossage_{i}.html\'\n            with open(artist_page_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                f.write(response.text)\n            print(f\'✓ Artist page saved to: {artist_page_file}\')\n            \n            # Parse for artist information\n            soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, \'html.parser\')\n            page_text = soup.get_text()\n            \n            # Look for biographical information\n            if \'gossage\' in page_text.lower():\n                print(\'✓ Found Gossage-related content\')\n                \n                # Look for birth/death dates\n                date_patterns = [\n                    r\'(\\d{4})[-–](\\d{4})\',  # Birth-death years\n                    r\'born\\s+(\\d{4})\',      # Born year\n                    r\'b\\.\\s*(\\d{4})\',       # b. year\n                    r\'(\\d{4})[-–]present\',   # Born-present\n                ]\n                \n                for pattern in date_patterns:\n                    matches = re.findall(pattern, page_text, re.IGNORECASE)\n                    if matches:\n                        print(f\'Date information found: {matches}\')\n                        artist_info[\'dates\'] = matches\n                        break\n                \n                # Look for information about "The Pond" series\n                pond_indicators = [\'pond\', \'water\', \'reflection\', \'series\']\n                found_pond_refs = []\n                \n                for indicator in pond_indicators:\n                    if indicator.lower() in page_text.lower():\n                        found_pond_refs.append(indicator)\n                \n                if found_pond_refs:\n                    print(f\'Pond series indicators found: {found_pond_refs}\')\n                    artist_info[\'pond_references\'] = found_pond_refs\n                \n                # Look for exhibition or publication dates\n                year_pattern = r\'\\b(19|20)\\d{2}\\b\'\n                years_found = re.findall(year_pattern, page_text)\n                if years_found:\n                    recent_years = [int(year) for year in years_found if int(year) >= 1980]\n                    if recent_years:\n                        max_year = max(recent_years)\n                        min_year = min(recent_years)\n                        print(f\'Activity years found: {min_year}-{max_year}\')\n                        artist_info[\'activity_years\'] = (min_year, max_year)\n                        \n                        # Check if any work could be from August 2023 or earlier\n                        if max_year <= 2023:\n                            print(\'✓ Artist activity includes August 2023 or earlier period\')\n                            artist_info[\'meets_date_requirement\'] = True\n                        else:\n                            print(\'⚠ Most recent activity may be after August 2023\')\n                            artist_info[\'meets_date_requirement\'] = False\n            \n            # ===\')\nworkspace_files = [f for f in os.listdir(\'workspace\') if os.path.isfile(os.path.join(\'workspace\', f))]\nprint(f\'Found {len(workspace_files)} files in workspace:\')\nfor file in workspace_files:\n    file_path = os.path.join(\'workspace\', file)\n    file_size = os.path.getsize(file_path)\n    print(f\'  - {file}: {file_size:,} bytes\')\n\n# Look for any existing Federico Lauria research files\nlauria_files = [f for f in workspace_files if \'lauria\' in f.lower() or \'federico\' in f.lower()]\nif lauria_files:\n    print(f\'\\nFound {len(lauria_files)} existing Lauria-related files:\')\n    for file in lauria_files:\n        print(f\'  - {file}\')\nelse:\n    print(\'\\nNo existing Lauria-related files found\')\n\nheaders = {\n    \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/120.0.0.0 Safari/537.36\',\n    \'Accept\': \'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,image/webp,*/*;q=0.8\',\n    \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.9\',\n    \'Connection\': \'keep-alive\'\n}\n\nprint(\'\\n=== SEARCHING ACADEMIC DATABASES FOR FEDERICO LAURIA PUBLICATIONS ===\')\n\n# Search strategies for Federico Lauria publications around 2014\nsearch_strategies = [\n    {\n        \'name\': \'Google Scholar\',\n        \'base_url\': \'https://scholar.google.com/scholar\',\n        \'params\': {\n            \'q\': \'Federico Lauria desire intentionality deontic logic\',\n            \'as_ylo\': \'2013\',\n            \'as_yhi\': \'2015\'\n        }\n    },\n    {\n        \'name\': \'PhilPapers\',\n        \'base_url\': \'https://philpapers.org/s/Federico%20Lauria\',\n        \'params\': {}\n    },\n    {\n        \'name\': \'Academia.edu\',\n        \'base_url\': \'https://www.academia.edu/search\',\n        \'params\': {\n            \'q\': \'Federico Lauria philosophy desire\'\n        }\n    },\n    {\n        \'name\': \'ResearchGate\',\n        \'base_url\': \'https://www.researchgate.net/search\',\n        \'params\': {\n            \'q\': \'Federico Lauria\',\n            \'type\': \'publication\'\n        }\n    }\n]\n\nlauria_publications = []\n\nfor i, strategy in enumerate(search_strategies, 1):\n    print(f\'\\n--- Search Strategy {i}: {strategy["name"]} ---\')\n    \n    try:\n        # Construct search URL\n        if strategy[\'params\']:\n            param_string = \'&\'.join([f\'{k}={quote(str(v))}\' for k, v in strategy[\'params\'].items()])\n            search_url = f\'{strategy["base_url"]}?{param_string}\'\n        else:\n            search_url = strategy[\'base_url\']\n        \n        print(f\'Search URL: {search_url}\')\n        \n        # {len(results)} Google Scholar results\')\n                \n                for j, result in enumerate(results[:5], 1):\n                    # Extract title\n                    title_elem = result.find(\'h3\') or result.find(\'a\')\n                    if title_elem:\n                        title_link = title_elem.find(\'a\') if title_elem.name != \'a\' else title_elem\n                        title = title_link.get_text().strip() if title_link else title_elem.get_text().strip()\n                        url = title_link.get(\'href\') if title_link else None\n                        \n                        # Extract authors and metadata\n                        result_text = result.get_text()\n                        \n                        # Look for author information\n                        author_patterns = [\n                            r\'F\\s+Lauria\',\n                            r\'Federico\\s+Lauria\',\n                            r\'Lauria,?\\s+F\',\n                            r\'Lauria,?\\s+Federico\'\n                        ]\n                        \n                        author_found = any(re.search(pattern, result_text, re.IGNORECASE) for pattern in author_patterns)\n                        \n                        # Extract year\n                        year_match = re.search(r\'\\b(201[3-5])\\b\', result_text)\n                        year = year_match.group(1) if year_match else None\n                        \n                        print(f\'  {j}. "{title}"\')\n                        if year:\n                            print(f\'     Year: {year}\')\n                        if author_found:\n                            print(f\'     ✓ Federico Lauria identified as author\')\n                        if url:\n                            print(f\'     URL: {url}\')\n                        \n                        # Check if this looks like a relevant Lauria publication\n                        if author_found and any(term in result_text.lower() for term in [\'desire\', \'intentionality\', \'deontic\']):\n                            lauria_publications.append({\n                                \'title\': title,\n                                \'year\': year,\n                                \'url\': url,\n                                \'source\': \'Google Scholar\',\n                                \'relevance_score\': \'High\',\n                                \'text_snippet\': result_text[:300]\n                            })\n                            print(f\'     *** HIGH RELEVANCE PUBLICATION IDENTIFIED ***\')\n            \n            elif \'philpapers.org\' in search_url:\n                # PhilPapers results\n                # Look for publication entries\n                pub_links = soup.find_all(\'a\', href=lambda x: x and \'/rec/\' in x)\n                print(f\'Found {len(pub_links)} PhilPapers publication links\')\n                \n                for j, link in enumerate(pub_links[:5], 1):\n                    title = link.get_text().strip()\n                    url = urljoin(\'https://philpapers.org\', link.get(\'href\'))\n                    \n                    # Look for surrounding context\n                    parent = link.parent\n                    context = parent.get_text() if parent else \'\'\n                    \n                    print(f\'  {j}. "{title}"\')\n                    print(f\'     URL: {url}\')\n                    \n                    if \'lauria\' in context.lower():\n                        lauria_publications.append({\n                            \'title\': title,\n                            \'url\': url,\n                            \'source\': \'PhilPapers\',\n                            \'relevance_score\': \'High\',\n                            \'context\': context[:200]\n                        })\n                        print(f\'     *** LAURIA PUBLICATION IDENTIFIED ***\')\n            \n            elif \'academia.edu\' in search_url:\n                # Academia.edu results\n                # Look for work titles\n                work_links = soup.find_all(\'a\', href=lambda x: x and \'/papers/\' in x if x else False)\n                print(f\'Found {len(work_links)} Academia.edu work links\')\n                \n                for j, link in enumerate(work_links[:5], 1):\n                    title = link.get_text().strip()\n                    url = urljoin(\'https://www.academia.edu\', link.get(\'href\'))\n                    \n                    print(f\'  {j}. "{title}"\')\n                    print(f\'     URL: {url}\')\n                    \n                    if \'lauria\' in title.lower() or \'federico\' in title.lower():\n                        lauria_publications.append({\n                            \'title\': title,\n                            \'url\': url,\n                            \'source\': \'Academia.edu\',\n                            \'relevance_score\': \'Medium\'\n                        })\n                        print(f\'     *** POTENTIAL LAURIA WORK IDENTIFIED ***\')\n        \n        elif response.status_code == 403:\n            print(\'❌ Access forbidden - site may be blocking automated requests\')\n        else:\n            print(f\'❌ Request failed with status {response.status_code}\')\n        \n        time.sleep(3)  # Rate limiting between searches\n        \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\'Error with {strategy["name"]} search: {str(e)}\')\n\nprint(\'\\n=== SEARCHING FOR SECONDARY SOURCES AND CITATIONS ===\') \n\n# Search for secondary sources that might mention Lauria\'s dissertation or footnote 397\nsecondary_search_terms = [\n    \'Federico Lauria dissertation desire\',\n    \'"footnote 397" Federico Lauria\',\n    \'Lauria philosophy desire intentionality citation\',\n    \'Federico Lauria 2014 dissertation review\'\n]\n\nsecondary_sources = []\n\nfor i, search_term in enumerate(secondary_search_terms, 1):\n    print(f\'\\n--- Secondary Source Search {i}: "{search_term}" ---\')\n    \n    try:\n        # Use Google search for secondary sources\n        google_url = f\'https://www.google.com/search?q={quote(search_term)}\'\n        print(f\'Search URL: {google_url}\')\n        \n        response = requests.get(google_url, headers=headers, timeout=20)\n        print(f\'Response status: {response.status_code}\')\n        \n        if response.status_code == 200:\n            # Save response\n            response_file = f\'workspace/secondary_search_{i}.html\'\n            with open(response_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                f.write(response.text)\n            print(f\'✓ Response saved to: {response_file}\')\n            \n            # Parse for relevant results\n            soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, \'html.parser\')\n            \n            # Look for search result containers\n            result_containers = soup.find_all(\'div\', class_=lambda x: x and (\'g\' in x or \'result\' in x))\n            if not result_containers:\n                # Save the PDF\n        pdf_file = \'workspace/lauria_logic_of_liver_2014.pdf\'\n        with open(pdf_file, \'wb\') as f:\n            f.write(response.content)\n        \n        file_size = os.path.getsize(pdf_file)\n        print(f\'✓ PDF saved successfully: {pdf_file}\')\n        print(f\'File size: {file_size:,} bytes ({file_size/1024/1024:.2f} MB)\')\n        \n        # Try to extract text from PDF\n        try:\n            print(\'\\nAttempting to extract text from PDF...\')\n            from langchain_community.document_loaders import PyPDFLoader\n            \n            loader = PyPDFLoader(pdf_file)\n            pages = loader.load_and_split()\n            \n            print(f\'✓ PDF loaded successfully with {len(pages)} pages\')\n            \n            # Combine all pages into full text\n            full_pdf_text = \'\\n\\n\'.join([page.page_content for page in pages])\n            \n            # Save extracted text\n            text_file = \'workspace/lauria_logic_of_liver_2014_extracted_text.txt\'\n            with open(text_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                f.write(full_pdf_text)\n            \n            print(f\'✓ Extracted PDF text saved to: {text_file}\')\n            print(f\'Total extracted text length: {len(full_pdf_text):,} characters\')\n            \n            # Search for footnote patterns\n            footnote_patterns = [\n                r\'footnote\\s+\\d+\',\n                r\'note\\s+\\d+\', \n                r\'\\[\\d+\\]\',\n                r\'\\(\\d+\\)\',\n                r\'\\b\\d{2,3}\\b\'  # 2-3 digit numbers that could be footnote references\n            ]\n            \n            footnote_matches = []\n            for pattern in footnote_patterns:\n                matches = re.findall(pattern, full_pdf_text, re.IGNORECASE)\n                footnote_matches.extend(matches)\n            \n            if footnote_matches:\n                print(f\'Found {len(footnote_matches)} footnote-like patterns:\')\n                unique_matches = list(set(footnote_matches))\n                for match in unique_matches[:10]:  # Show first 10\n                    print(f\'  - {match}\')\n                \n                # Check specifically for 397 or similar high numbers\n                high_numbers = [match for match in unique_matches if any(char.isdigit() and int(\'\'.join(filter(str.isdigit, match))) > 300) for char in match)]\n                if high_numbers:\n                    print(f\'\\n*** HIGH FOOTNOTE NUMBERS FOUND: {high_numbers} ***\')\n                    if \'397\' in str(footnote_matches):\n                        print(\'*** FOOTNOTE 397 PATTERN DETECTED! ***\')\n            \n            # Search for literary/artistic terms\n            literary_terms = [\n                \'painting\', \'artwork\', \'art\', \'visual\', \'image\',\n                \'literary\', \'literature\', \'poem\', \'poetry\', \'novel\',\n                \'quotation\', \'quote\', \'reference\', \'citation\',\n                \'pond\', \'thoreau\', \'walden\', \'series\', \'untitled\',\n                \'museum\', \'gallery\', \'exhibition\', \'artist\'\n            ]\n            \n            found_literary_terms = []\n            for term in literary_terms:\n                if term in text_lower:\n                    # Count occurrences\n                    count = text_lower.count(term)\n                    found_literary_terms.append((term, count))\n            \n            if found_literary_terms:\n                print(f\'\\n*** LITERARY/ARTISTIC TERMS FOUND: ***\')\n                for term, count in found_literary_terms:\n                    print(f\'  - "{term}": {count} occurrence(s)\')\n                    \n                    # Extract context around these terms\n                    for match in re.finditer(re.escape(term), text_lower):\n                        start = max(0, match.start() - 150)\n                        end = min(len(full_pdf_text), match.end() + 150)\n                        context = full_pdf_text[start:end]\n                        print(f\'\\n    Context for "{term}": ...{context}...\')\n                        break  # Show only first context for each term\n            else:\n                print(\'\\n⚠ No obvious literary/artistic terms found in PDF text\')\n            \n            # Search for specific patterns that might indicate artistic references\n            artistic_patterns = [\n                r\'"[^"]+"\\s*\\([^)]+\\)\',  # "Title" (Author/Year)\n                r\'[A-Z][a-z]+\\s+[A-Z][a-z]+\\s*\\([^)]+\\)\',  # Author Name (Year)\n                r\'series\\s+[A-Z][^.!?]*\',  # "series" followed by title\n                r\'untitled[^.!?]*\',  # "untitled" references\n                r\'from\\s+the\\s+series[^.!?]*\'  # "from the series" pattern\n            ]\n            \n            artistic_matches = []\n            for pattern in artistic_patterns:\n                matches = re.findall(pattern, full_pdf_text, re.IGNORECASE)\n                artistic_matches.extend(matches)\n            \n            if artistic_matches:\n                print(f\'\\n*** ARTISTIC REFERENCE PATTERNS FOUND: ***\')\n                for i, match in enumerate(artistic_matches[:5], 1):  # Show first 5\n                    print(f\'  {i}. {match}\')\n                    \n                    # Check if this matches our "The Pond" series pattern\n                    if any(term in match.lower() for term in [\'pond\', \'series\', \'untitled\']):\n                        print(f\'      *** POTENTIAL MATCH WITH "THE POND" SERIES PATTERN! ***\')\n            \n            # Search for bibliography or references section\n            bibliography_indicators = [\'bibliography\', \'references\', \'works cited\', \'sources\']\n            bibliography_found = False\n            \n            for indicator in bibliography_indicators:\n                if indicator in text_lower:\n                    print(f\'\\n*** BIBLIOGRAPHY SECTION FOUND: "{indicator}" ***\')\n                    \n                    # Save comprehensive analysis\n            pdf_analysis = {\n                \'analysis_timestamp\': time.strftime(\'%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S\'),\n                \'pdf_file\': pdf_file,\n                \'text_file\': text_file,\n                \'total_pages\': len(pages),\n                \'total_characters\': len(full_pdf_text),\n                \'footnote_patterns_found\': len(footnote_matches),\n                \'unique_footnote_patterns\': list(set(footnote_matches)),\n                \'literary_terms_found\': found_literary_terms,\n                \'artistic_patterns_found\': artistic_matches,\n                \'bibliography_section_found\': bibliography_found,\n                \'potential_footnote_397_connection\': \'397\' in str(footnote_matches),\n                \'potential_pond_series_connection\': any(\'pond\' in str(match).lower() for match in artistic_matches)\n            }\n            \n            analysis_file = \'workspace/lauria_pdf_comprehensive_analysis.json\'\n            with open(analysis_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                json.dump(pdf_analysis, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)\n            \n            print(f\'\\n✓ Comprehensive PDF analysis saved to: {analysis_file}\')\n            \n        except ImportError:\n            print(\'⚠ PyPDFLoader not available - PDF saved but text extraction skipped\')\n            print(\'PDF file can be manually reviewed for footnote 397 and literary references\')\n        except Exception as pdf_error:\n            print(f\'❌ PDF text extraction error: {str(pdf_error)}\')\n            print(\'PDF file saved but text extraction failed\')\n    \n    elif response.status_code == 200:\n        print(\'✓ Received response but content is not PDF format\')\n        # Oddie - Value and desires (Oxford Handbook of Value Theory, 2015)\\n\\n\')\n                for i, context in enumerate(unique_contexts, 1):\n                    f.write(f\'--- Context {i} ---\\n\')\n                    f.write(context)\n                    f.write(\'\\n\\n\')\n            \n            print(f\'\\n✓ Lauria contexts saved to: {contexts_file}\')\n        \n        else:\n            print(f\'⚠ No Lauria references found in {books_file}\')\nelse:\n    print(\'No existing Google Books files found - attempting fresh access\')\n    \n    #
